meam thus whyle ſayd byrd began ſtrongely crye ſay ¶o frenſſhe man ſayeſt thou frenſſhe man ſayſt thou kyng hys companye wente folowed byrde whyche conduyted vnto ryght wayr whyche loſt day fore ſomme pylgryms ſayd ſame contreye ſuche byrdes ſo doyng whan charles hys grete puyſſaunce nyghe theyr enemyes moche troubled theyr comyng cryſten lordes gretely reioyſed theyr comyng wythoute ceſſyng reſted tyl trcouerd contreye cryſten men expelled alle paynyms whyche moche redounded hym grete honour vyctorye retournyng demaunded themperour conſtantynoble lycence departe patryarkes archepereſtes thempe ¶of relyques themperour charles brought fro conſtantynoble fro holy londe myracles doo capitulo iij whan themperour conſtantynople patryarke iheruſalem knewe charles wold take thynge good aforſayd holy paſſyon gloryous roſurrexyon aſſone prayed moment crowne began floryſſhe meruayllous ſwete odour yſſued floures ſoo ryȝt delycyous eche man ſuppoſed hys veſtementes clothyng comen oute heuen ¶thēne thys daniel took ſharpe knyf kuttyng wel puryfyed cutte ſaid crowne cuttyng alwaye ſayd crowne flouryſſhed odour ſmellyd habundantly floures charles put parte repoſytorye lytel coffre put thornes crowne wept ſo habundantlye whan wende haue gyuen tharchebyſſhop ebroin floures wythdrewe hys honde ſuppoſed ſayd ebroin holden hys honde ayer houyng myracle abode ſelf ſpace grete houre whan fraunce baptyſed deſcendyng purpoos vnto kynge charles whome may wel recoūted valyaūce hym hys baron whych named called pyeres fraūce whome behauyng ſhal make mencion ſhal mowe cōceyue trouthe like whyche kyng alexandrye helde vnder hym contree babylone vnto rede ſee lord rouſſye coulleygne ouer vnder hym iheruſalem reteyned holy ſepulcre lord iheſu cryſt hys grete puyſſaūce entred tyme rome dyd moche euyl bare awaye holy crowne lord holy naylles relyques ynoughe whome thys book ſhal thende recoūte recouerd called fyerabras alexandrye whyche many warres bataylles maad mormyonde bytwene paynyms thexcerſyte charles thys fyerabras moche dyſſolute came rydyng grete furour fynde ſōme criſten man fyght ayenſt hym came vnto lyces kynge charles moche furyous eſchauffed ſhold fyght al armed wel fournyſſhed wepen ryght euyl contente fonde perſone whome myght fyght nygh vnto lyces went beholde armes af themperour charles whyche aygle ſhynyng ſware mahommet god myȝt wold neuer departe tyll foughten made batayll ſomme cryſten man ſeeyng man cam hym began crpe hye voys kyng parys coward oute hardyneſſe ſende iuſte ayenſt ſomme thy baron fraunce mooſt ſtronge moſte hardy rolland olyuer thyer • ogyer danoys ſwere god mahon ſhal refuſe vnto nombre vj vij ſhal receyued yf thou make reffuſe thys demaunde promyſe tofore nyȝt thou ſhalt aſſaylled dyſcomfyted ſhal ſmyte thy heed meſchaunt withoute ony fayllyng ſhal lede rolland olyuer vnhappy meſchaunt caytyfs oultragyouſly folyly euyl olde haſt enpryſed come iij thys contreye wherfro thou ſhalt haue cauſe haſtely departe theſe wordes ſemblable ſpoken fyerabras wente hym vnto ſhadowe tree laye dyſarmed hym armes whyche cladde bonde hors vnto tree whan thus eaſe began crye hye voys charlemayn kyng parys art thou whome haue thys day ſo ofte called wythoute lenger delaye ſende iuſte ayenſt rolland olyuer thou makeſt ſo grete counte ſo valyaunte ogyer danoys haue herde preyſed yf perauenture one dare come allone hardyly late come two thre foure mooſt valyaunteſt courageous hardy wel armed yf four dare come late come fyue vnto nombre vi mooſt valyaunteſt thyn excerſyte ſhal refuſe thynke retorne tyl confuſed deſtroyed ye ſure ſhal neuer reproche fugytyf ony frenſſhe man lyuyng haue tofore put deth valyaunce perſone ten kynges grete puyſſaunce coude reſyſte ageynſt ſtrengthe wyſe ¶how rychard normandye ſayd charles maner man fyerabras ca iij aſſone fyerabras fynyſſhed hys wordes emperour charles whyche wel herde hym meruaylled moche hys langage demaunded rychard normandye turke ſo cryed wyth ſoo hye voys vpon valyaunce hys perſone kyng charles ſayd haue wel herkened hath ſaid ſhal fayle fyght ayenſt vj mooſt valyaunteſt myn excerſyte whome rychard duke normandye anſuerd syr kyng thys man meruayllous ryche one ſtrengeſt borne moder ſaraſyn ſo grete fyerſte ne preyſeth kyng ne erle ne none perſone worl • ¶whan charles vnderſtood hym began clawe • eed ſware saynt de • y fraunce ſhold ete ne neuer drynke tyl one pyeres fraunce ſhold goo iuſte ageynſt hym demaunded rychard normandye thys popnyt named ¶rychard anſwerd ſyr emperour paynym nameth hym ſelf fyerabras moche redoubte hath done moche harme cryſten men hath ſlayn pope hanged abbottes monkes nonnes hath deffuled chyrches ¶and hath robbed taken awaye holy crowne lord many rely • ues whome ye take grete payne holdeth iheruſalem grete ſubgectyon holy ſepulcre wherin god buryed wherupon charles anſuerd thys thou haſt ſayd āgry knowe thou certayn ſhalle neuer haue ioye tyll deſyre accomplyſſhed vaynquyſſhed fayt al frenſſhe men commoeued troubled ther one preſented hym goo hym whan charles ſawe noo perſone courage goo fyght ageynſt thys geaunt fyerabras ſayd rolland dere neuewe praye thou dyſpoſe taſſaylle thys turke thou doo thy deuoyr ¶of anſwer roulland emperour ſodeynlye capitulo iiij whan themperour charles ſpoken thus curtoyſly vnto neuewe rolland folyly wythoute reaſon rolland anſwerd hym thus fayt vncle ſpeke neuer therof leuer ye confuſed dyſmembred ſhold take armes hors iuſte lyke ye ſay laſt day ſo nyghe taken paynyms ſay moo fyfty thouſand yonge knyghtes bare burthen ſuffred many mortal ſtrokes whych olyuer felowe quaſi hurt vnto deth yf ye ſocoured v hole deſtructyon v thende whan repayred lodgys take reſte euen whan ye wel dronken ye maad auaunte openlye olde auncyent knygytes whyche ye brouȝt wyth ayde v moche better borne fayt armes ſtronge bataylle yonge knyghtes ¶and euery man knoweth wel euenyng affebled wery trauaylle took day faders ſoule euyll ſayd ¶and ſhal knowen olde auncient knyghtes ſhal bere god whyche ought haue al ſubgectyon noo yonge man companye euer ſhal fauour loue yf take vpon hym iuſte ageynſt paynym alſo ſone roulland ſpoken worde themperour hys vncle hauyng moche iudignaciō therat ſmote hym thwarte vyſage wyth hys ryght gannteto • hys noſe breſte blood habundauntly ſtroke thenne roulland grete furye ſette honde hys ſwerde whan ſawe hys blood ſmeton hys vncle yf lette preſente whan charles ſawe tencyon roullaud meruayllouſly abaſſhed ſayd god heuen wold haue thought ſhold haue vylonye rolland neuew whyche knytte gyder one fayth ayenſt aduerſaryes cometh rennyng ageynſt wyth affectyon mortal mooſt nexte blood lignage preſent ſonner ſhold ſ • coure ony ¶now beſeche god croſſe ſuffred paſſyon day punyſſhed worthy ſaid grete furour comaunded frenſſhe men ſayd anone take ye hym ſhall neuer ete tyl delyuerd deth whan frenſſhe men vnderſtood commaundemnt charles haue accomplyſſhed one loked vpon ſee wold ſette fyrſt honde vpon hym whan roulland ſawe fayt withdrewe hym litel parte wyth hys ſwerde hys honde cryeng hyghe voys ſayenge theym yf ye wyſe holde ſtylle make vowe god yf ony moeue come ſhal make hys heed two partes wherfore one durſt ne ſoo hardy meue ageynſt hym malyce ryght ſory euyll contente theyr debate vpon noble ogier came ſwetelye roulland ſayd hym syr roulland ſemeth ye doo wel angre thus vncle emperour •• reaſon ye ought aboue alle loue defende alſo ſupporte roulland anſwerd whyche thenne refrayned hys ire syr ogyer promyſe lytel fayt determyned grete oultrage wythoute aduys enclyned wherof ſory repenteth ¶how kyng charles roulland repreued anctour ſomwhat excuſed vpon debate aforeſayd ca v vpon debate perour rolland hys • euewe wyll lytyl tarye ſpelle fyrſt kyng charles whyche haſte iuſtuicte ſyth thyn infancye alle ſeyences ful maners digne commemoracyon whiche kneweſt conſtaunce auncyents mutabylyte yonge peple ſaydeſt thou euene auncyent olde knyghtes warre day borne better thā yonge knyȝtes thou kneweſt well olyuer gretely hurte hys valyaunce ſuche wyſe kepeth hys bedde alſo rolland thy neuewe borne grete burthen bataylle yf ſpoken folily thou oughteſt haue ſupported hys fyrſt moeuyng whiche puyſſaunce man yf thou haddeſt taken aduys word ſayth vindictam differ donec pertranſcat furor ſay thou oughteſt dylate thy vengeaunce tyll furour paſſed thou ſholdeſt haue ſmyton rolland sythe whan ſayd euyl wythout aduys grete dyſcreſcyon thou ſmoteſt hym ſemblably wythout aduys drewe hys ſwerde ayenſt though thou haddeſt ſmeton hym thou myghteſt well haue reprehēded hym offēce thou oughteſt remembre eccleſyaſtes whyche ſayth richilagas operibus iniurie whan man receyueth wronge iniurye good doo whyche may doo alſo whan perſone hath wel doon hys deuoyr hym whome ought haue hys thanke preyſyng blamed ſoo moche euyll contente wrothe hys fayt reputed nought lyke wyſe rolland whyche thought haue alowed preyſed grete deuoyr dyd emperour ſayd tholde knyghtes doon better yonge wyl retorne rolland whiche haſt ſo noble fro whens cometh ſuche audacyte ſpeke ageynſt thyn vncle whyche hath allwaye doon ſo wel hys werkes worthy remembred hym emperour kynge fraunce lord ſo grete cremeur thyn vncle taken debate anſuerd outrageouſly reaſon thou oughteſt ſuffer hym yf ſmote wyth hys gauntelet maner correctyon oughteſt thou drawe thy ſwerde hym thou haſt rememberaunce obeyſſaunce yſaac whyche hys fader thou aduyſed thys thappoſtle ſaith ye yōge men kepe courage put furour therof exerſi • e yf emperour hys dyſporte preyſed thauncyent knyghtes yet ſayd thou haddeſt doon wel ¶and saynt poule ſayth hys epyſtle man ſhold repreue hym aūcyent hym ſelf man ought entretene ſupporte hym fader dede ſuche perſone reputeth iniurye hym ſayd lytel ne yf hurte pacyent wherfore good thynke ſpeke gladly doo ne ſay thynge yf good ¶how olyuer dyſpoſed fyght ageynſt fyerabras wythſtondyng hurt many woedes capitulo vj moche wroth charles wyth rolland hys neuewe ſayd hys peres fraunce lordes dyuers thoughtes neuewe rolland whyche wold haue iniuryed perſone whome affyaūce ony man lyuyng wote neuer whome ought loue ne whome ought hate yet furthermore haue noo man preſent iuſte ageynſt thys paynym hath chalenged ¶thenne aroos vp tofore hym naymes duc bauyers whych ſayd kyng syr emperour praye requyre ye leue theſe wordes noyouſes alle ſhal wel another ſhal goo iuſte ageynſt ſaraſyn neuertheles kyng grete thought none wold goo ne take hym ¶incontynente tydynges debate charles rolland brought olyuer whyche another place ſeek hys bedde alſo fyerabras comen perſone preſent wyth kynge iuſte ayenſt hym hereupon noble erle olyuer replenyſſhed wyth noble courage wyth ardaunt deſyre playſe kynge whan herde theſe tydynges aroos oute hys bedde began ſtratche ſtrayne hys armes fele yf poſſyble hym bere armes thus dooyng woū de began newely opene blood ſprange oute dyſtreſſe ¶and wythſtondyng alle ſette moche therby grete loue deſyre kyng dyd bynde hys woundes beſte wyſe myght ſayd garin ſquyer ſhold brynge hym hys armes wold arme hym goo iuſt ayenſt ſareſyn whome garyn ſayd ſyr olyuer thonour god take pyte owne perſone thynketh ye wil willyngly ſlee ſelf olyuer ſayd hym commaundement man ought tarye ſeche hys honour auauncement renommee wyth good ryght may employe ſelf ſerue prynce ſynguler lord ſythe ſee noo frenſſhe man auaunceth hym ſhall faylle poynte comyn prouerbe ſayth nede man knoweth hys frende anone brynge myn armes wythoute taryeng ſo olyuer dyd doo arme hym ſayd garyn hys ſquyer whiche ſette legge harnays hys hawberke hys helme harnays neceſſarye whan alle furnyſhed took hys ſwerde named hautrelere whyche ſwerde moche loued brought hym hys hors mooſt ſpecyall loved whyche named ferraunt deſpaygne whan brought tofore hym alle ſadled brydled ioly gentyl olyuer ſprange ſadle wythoute ſettyng foot ſtyrop ſette hys ſhelde hys eaſe hys honde myghty ſpere ſharpe whych garyn took hym ſmote hors wyth ſpores ſo harde leepyng maad hys hors bowe vnder hym good ſyght ſee olyuer horſback wyth moche fyers countenaunce preſente byſought iheſu cryſt redemar ſhold take hym hys kepyng day ſhold fyght ageynſt mooſt ſtrong mooſt fyers paynym euer born moder euer thys world fyerabras alexandrye ſone admyral ballant ſpayne whome ſhalle ſee playſyr god termynacyon ¶he beyng thus horſback grete poynt vpon hys vyſage vpon body maad ſygne croſſe name iheſus commaunded hym ſelf wylle god whyche day ſhold hym comforte ayde hys good entencyon euery man byſeen knowen firſt hole hys body grete feat armes ſo rode forth vnto lyces themperour charles duc naymes guyllam de ſcot gerard de mondydyer ogyer danoys wyth baron freunce emonge alle rolland moche ſorouful wordes ayenſt vncle kyng gladly wolde haue doo bataylle yf wythſayed tofore kyng whan requyred thus olyuer beyng ſeen tofore charles moche alowed preyſed one moche affectuouſly byholden ſaid olyuer put doun helme byhelde lodgyce kyng reuerently came ſalewed hym ſayd hym noble emperour puyſſaūt redoubted ſynguler lord beſeche ye know wel ben iij yeres paſt haue ſeruyce haue rewarde ne wage ſupplye al myn herte ye wyll rewarde wyth yefte ſhal deſyre kyng anſuerd olyuer noble erle aſſure fayth ſhal wyth good wylle aſſone ſhall fraunce neyther cyte nigh ne caſtel ye wyl haue ne none thyng poſſyble fayſyble ſhal denyed syr kyng ſaid olyuer comen demaunde ſuche thynge demaunde requyre bataylle ayenſte paynym ſo oute meſure thys houce graunte alle goodes ſeruyces yefte quyte whan frenſſhe men herde olyuer abaſſhed hys proweſſe eche loked ſaid emonge ſaynt marie hath olyuer founden wyyche hurt quaſi deth wyl goo fyght bataylle olyuer anſwerd charles thou haſt loſte thy wytte thou know eſt wel wyth ſpere heed ſquare ſharpe thou haſt hurte wounded mortally thou wylt abandon •• thy ſelf gretter daunger mortall beware retorne take thy reſte 〈◊〉 well noo thynge ſhall ſuffre fayte ſythen thou arte preſently helthe body vpon thys poynte aroos ganellon andrewe traytres dyd 〈◊〉 laſte look ſhall make mencyon ¶and oanellon ſayd syr kyng ye haue ordeygned fraunce whyche ij v iug • ought holden ſo ij iuge ordeyne olyuer ſhalle goo doo bataylle wherfore kyng ful maltalente wyth coloure chaunged anſwerd ganellon thou arte euyl dyſpoſycyon wythoute ſpekyng whyche honourable sythe ſo ſhal doo bataylle may none otherwyſe dede ſwere trouth yf taken put deth al gold world ſhal ſaue thou ſhalt dye vylaynous deth ſhall deſtroye thy lygnage syr emperour ſayd ganellon god lady kepe trayter ſayd hym ſelf ſecretly god forbede euer olyuer retorne haue hys heed ſmyton whan themperour ſawe myght gaynſaye olyuer ſhold goo bataylle ayenſt fyerabras ſayd praye god fyrmamente gyue grace wel thou mayſt retorne wyth ioye took hys ryght gloue threwe olyuer receyued wyth grete deſyre wylle thankyng hym ryght humbly takyng leue al moche ſwetely ¶hoth olyuer requyred fader reyner ſhold fyght wyth geaunt al went forth ca vij whan olyuer lycenced goo doo hys bataylle redy departe reyner gene hys fader came kyng grete compaſſyon kneled doun hys foot ſayd syr kyng crye mercy hane pyte ſotte ſay ye wyl al dyſcomforte whan ſee ſone gooth perdycyon ſeeyng daunger hys perſone ſay alſo ye take pyte preſumptuous yongthe hys deſyre ouer couetous body woūded daūgerouſly ye knowe wel man hurte ſo ſore hath loſte hys blood may wel endure bataylle reyner loſte hys payne kyng gyuen hym hys gloue ſygne lycence wythſtondyng theſe wordes doubted thyng ſhold wel hys deuoyr valyauntly yet ageyn reyner requyred kyng ſayd syr kyng thonour hym v deyed croſſe ſuffre ſone iuſt ala whan ſhal haue loſt ſone ſhal become ye may wel fynde take thys bataylle honde thempero ur charles anſwerd reyner ye knowe wel may gaynſaye haue hym graunted ſygne lycēce haue gyuen hym gloue wherof olyuer contente thenne olyuer ſayd wyth hye voys tofore alle people syr kyng alle ye baron beſeche alle yefte requyre yf haue meſpryſed myſdoon dede worde ony ayenſt name god ye pardōne whan frenſſh men herde hym ſo ſpeke none wepte tenderly ſoo takyng hys leue wyth ſtandard reyſed kyng bleſſyd hym makyng ſygne croſſe wepyng comaūded hym kepyng fader ſone holy ghoſt ¶how olyuer ſpake fyerabras whyche ſette noo thynge hym diſputacions capitulo viij olyuer departed rode forth hys waye taryed tyl cam fyerabras al vnarmed laye ſhadowe whan olyuer areſonned hym paynym torned heed ayenſt hym dayned vnnethe loke hym ſetted nought hym cauſe ſo lytel ſtature regarde fyerabras thenne olyuer ſaid ſaraſyn awake thou thou haſt thys day ſo ofte called v come hyther praye thou telle thy name fyerabras anſuerd hym mahoun god whome owe honour mooſt ryche man world borne fyerabras alexandrye named thou knowe dyd doo deſtroye rome cyte ſhewe pope many bare awaye relyques founde ye take grete payne laboure receuer furthermore holde iheruſalem fayre 〈◊〉 ſepulere whych god reſted olyuer anſuerd fayth haue gladl • herde ſay whyche thou haſt ſayd yf trouth thou haſt ſayd certayn thou mayſt repute thy ſelf well vnhappy myſchaunt wythout ••• kyng make redy 〈◊〉 ſeeſt thou yonder frenſſhe men doo thynge byholde v wherfore depeſſ • e god whome byleue ſhalle ſmyte 〈◊〉 thou lye •• whan fyerabras herde ſpake ſoo hardyly began lawhe ſayd wel admeruaylled fro whens cometh ſuche preſum • ſpeke ſo haſ • yly touche ſhal remeue fro hen tyll knowe thou arte lygnage whan thou haſt tolde thy name thou ſhalt ſee armed olyuer ſuerd hym paynem know thou trouthe nyght thou ſhalt knowe ſendeth charles emperour redoubted lord conſecracion thy body ſaluacyon thy ſoule thou leue creaunce thy god mahoun ydolles whyche ben abuſyon decrepcyon whych haue neyther wyt •• ne reaſon ne feelyng ne good vnderſtondyng wherfore thou enclyne conſente thynke fro hen forth byleue god almyghty holy trynyte fader ſone holy ghooſt iij perſones one eſſence one wylle whyche hath made heuen erthe al dwelleth whyche ſaluacion wold borne vyrgyn marie whan thou ſhalt haue byleue wyth holy ſacrament bapteſme vpon eſtablyſſhed thou mayſt come glorye eternal yf thou lyke haue taught redy doo bataylle ayenſt two thynges thou muſt doo one fyrſt thou departe oute thys contree ouercomen thyng thou muſt come fyght ayenſt tenhaunce thy body ſuſteyne thy fals la • de fyerabras anſwerd ſomeuer thou art • thon arte ouer preſumptuous haue intencyon fyght ageynſt ſurely yf thou ſee fote wythoute armes thou ſhalt wel hardy yf thou tremble drede approche god whome thou byleueſt say man charlemayn long ſythe herde hym fyrſt preyſed redoubted many contrees alſo may haue tydynges rolland olyuer ogyer danoys gerarde de mondydyer trouthe wold fayn acqueynted olyuer anſuerd paynym vpon thou demaundeſt telle charles themperour ſo grete mayſtre man world may compare hym wel baluer hys perſone hys counceyl hys maners hys puyſſaunce rycheſſes innumerable regarde hys neuewe rolland wythoute pere olyuer lytel laſſe frenſſhe men emonge al people humayn balyaunte men thyſe wordes haue noo place depeſſhe arme god byleue yf thou auaunce ſhalle ſmyte wyth thys ſwerde ſtele fyerabras began lyfte vp hys heed ſayd god mahōmet yf thought ſhold dyſhonour ſhold ſmyte thy heed olyuer anſuerd praye leue thys pletyng euen thou ſhalt knowe certeyn haue entencyon plunge ſwerde thy bely vpon fyerabras wroth ſo moche noble reſted hys heed vpon hys ſheld ſayd olyuer ſe •• te therby praye bell thy name thy lygnage olyuer ſayd hym name garyn borne perrogort ſone man called aoſue whyche came day fraunce adouted knyght noble kyng charles ordryned defende hys ryght alſo fyght ayenſt wherfor conclude wythoute taryeng arme take thy hors redy doo bataylle yf thou ſoo hardy abyde fyerabras wold conſente bataylle hym thought olyuer litel iuſte ayenſt hym ſayd hym garyn demaunde wherfore comen hyther rolland ne olyuer gerard ogyer whyche ſo grede renōmee haue herd ſay olyuer anſuerd cauſe wherfore comen ſette nought haue deſdayn come comen taketh noo regarde theyr intencyon ſhal bataylle ageynſt yf thou wylt abyde ſwere ſaynt petre appoſtle iheſu cryſt yf thou arme ſhal ſmyte deth wyth thys darte holde honde garyn anſwerd fyerabras ſhal ſay ſythe adoubed knyght iuſted neuer ayenſt kyng erle baron grete valure thou art departed bow hous ſay ſhold haue aded wyth ſhold ouer grete dyſhonour yf thou put deth good wylle knowe whych moche noble contente thou ſmyte ſhal falle doun therthe take thou hors ſhelde goo thou kyng charles ſay hym thou haſt vaynquyſſhed yf thys grete amytye thou oughteſe thye tyme contente ¶on whiche woodes olyuer coude haue pacyence ſayd hym thy ſayt lyeth noothynge wordes full folyſſhe preſumpſyon thys intencion byfore euenſonge tyme ſhal make thy hede free thy ſholdres none hare ne wylde beeſt aferde thou knoweſt comyn▪ prouerbe ſayth tyme ſpekyng tyme beyng ſtylle one one may reputed fool come depeſſhe haue ſayd ellys ſhal ſlee frrwbras anſwerd deſyre ne praye thynge thou ſende rolland olyuer one thother knyghtes rounde table yf one hardy come late come ij iij iiij attones ſhal refuſed makyng theſe deſputacyōs olyuer ſore hurte day fore woundes opened force rydyng chauffyng bledde ſore ſo fyerabras ſawe blood renne doun knee demaūded hym fro whens came blood ſoo renneth doun therthe trowe thou hurte olyuer ſayd hurte hors harde atte ſpore wherof blody fyerabras behelde ſawe hors anſwerd certes garyn thou ſayſt ſooth thou art hurte thy body know wel blood cometh doun thy knee ſee ſhal two flagon hangyng ſadle hors whyche full bawme conquered iij iheruſalem ſame whyche god enbawmed wyth whan taken doun fro croſſe layed hys graue hye goo drynke therof promyſe incontynent thou ſhalte hole thene thou ſhalt mowe defende wel wythoute daunger ¶olyuer anſuerd wold ſayd folye thenne fyerabras anſuerd fool wythoute reaſon myght happe repente hym ¶how many dyſputacyons olyuer ayded arme fyerabras ix meruayllous ſwerdes olyuer named name ca ix whan fyerabras long abyden lyeng wythoute aryſyng olyer ſalte vp ſayd garyn demaunde wythoute hydyng ſtrengthe rolland olyuer ſoo moche redoubted paynems gretenes ben olyuer anſwerd towchyng rolland lytel laſſe body courage right hardy fyght ſo chyualrous man lyuyng world lyke hym neuer faught yet ayenſt ony man world vaynquyſſhed hym olyuer thou mayſt wel apperceyue man moche ſemblable lyke ſame gretenes thenne ſayd fyerabras fayth owe god appollyn termagaunt thou telleſt thynge wherof moche abaſſhed yf ſuche foure thou telleſt wold refuſe ne leue tyl put deth ſwerde olyuer coude longer forbere ne haue pacyence vnto delayes fyerabras made redy ſmyte hym wherfore fyerabras ſayd hym thou wyll haue pycyon thyn owne perſone mahoun god yf aryſe take hors charles thy kyng ne alle thy goodes ſhal redeme thou ſhalt incontynente ſlayn onelye yf thou ſee tofore foot thou ſhalt moche corageous yf thou tremble fere ¶olyuer anſwerd thou haſt haunted ouer longe doo thyng whiche thou neuer ſaweſt thy lyue better ſpeke meſure ouer moche ſpekyng otherwyſe trouthe may brynge ſoone myſchyef herof fyerabras ſtrongely deſpyteous roos hys foot grete fyerſnes whyche comyn eſtymacyon xv foot longe yf wold haue bartyſed byleue iheſu cryſt ther neuer ſeen man valure whan foot grete dyſplayſyr cauſe valyaunte man iuſte ageynſt hym ſayd olyuer trouthe haue grete pyte thyn affaire nobleſſe courage ſee yet contente preſent tyme thou retorne ſende rolland olyuer ogyer gerard demondydyer expreſſely ſay olyuer ſhall paſſe thys auauntagarde tyl haue conquerd hym olyuer myght lenger abyde paynym yf hys honour ſymte hym dyuers tymes vnarmed whan muſt nedes fyght fyerabras called olyuer prayed hym wold helpe arme hym olyuer demaunded yf myght truſte hym fyerabras anſuerd helpe hardyly •• ere aſſure neuer whyle lyue ſhal traytour man lyuyng vpon promyſe olyuer dyd dyligēce arme hym took fyrſt lether arabye cladde hym therwyth hys cote habergeō ſtele wel boucled polyſſhed ſette hys heed helme garnyſſhed wyth precyous ſtones rychely wel conſydered facyon thys payny • n criſten man grete toyalte curtoſye bytwene whyche aſſembled make mortal warre eche flee yet dyd eche ſynguler ſeruyce fyrſt pay • ym grete pyte deſtroye olyuer hys pere ne egal regarde hys perſone parte whan ſawe hym hurte blood deſcende therthe wold haue gyuen hym precyous bawme semblably olyuer whan fonde hym dyſarmed ſlayne hym wythoute grete payne yf wold ſoo curtoys ayded arme hym ſhold fyȝt ayenſt hym ¶o grete loyalte nobleſſe bytwene whyche fayth creaunce contrarye ſuppoſe god ſhold wel pleaſed yf ſuche confyaunce emonge cryſten men ſo ful naturel nobleſſe retorne ageyn mater whan fyerabras wel armed thanked moche olyuer gyrde hys ſwerde named plouraunce arſon ſadyl tweyne one named baptyſme graba • n whyche ſwerdes maad ſuche wyſe ther none harnoys wold breke cutte ſondre wyl demaunde manyer made whyche haue founden wrytyng ¶on tyme thre brethern one fader engendred whome one named galaus munyfyeans thyrd called agniſiax theſe iij brethern made ix ſwerdes eche thre agniſiax thyrd brother maad ſwerde named bapteſme whiche pomel gold wel enameld alſo plourance graham whyche thre ſwerdes fyerabras haue ſayd munyficans brother made another ſwerde whyche named durandal whyche rolland called ſauuagnye cortan whyche og • er danoys ¶and galaus brother maad ſwerd named floberge another called haulte clere ioyouſe whyche charlemayn grete ſpecyalte theſe iij brethern aforeſayd ſmythes wrought ſayd ſwerdes thys poynte fyerabras mounted hors backe took hys two barylles hym ful bawme henge aboute necke ſhelde whiche heuy bended wyth yron ſtele meruayllous ſtrengthe myddle ſame ſhelde paynted hys god appollyn commaunded hym hys god took ſpere hys honde whyche ſharpe mortally heded ſtele meruaylle ſee corpulence ſayd paynym ſat hys hors named feraunt ſpayne grete thycke pommellyd whyche ſpecyal condycyon whan mayſter fyghtyng put grounde hys aduerſarye hors maad gretter warre wythout comparyſon hys mayſter thus beyng horſback fyerabras ſayd olyuer garyn gracyous curtoys yet admoneſte gentylneſſe thou haſt doon thou retorne without fyghtyng haue pyte thy valyaunte courage olyuer anſwerde alwaye thou ſpekeſt grete folye ſhal departe daunger dyſmembred thou weneſt make aferde helpe bleſſyd iheſus thys day ſhalt thou yelden deed lyuyng vnto charles emperour whan olyuer ſo ſpoken fyerabras meruaylouſly abaſſhed thys man wold lete menace maad hym wold haue bataylle ayenſt hym ſayd hym thou art cryſten man haſt grete fayth myſteryes ordeyned coniure fonte iij whyche thou baptyſed fayth thou haſt gyuen croſſe wheron thy god henge naylled loyalte thou oweſt charles themperour rolland pyeres fraūce thou ſay telle veryte thy ryght name thy lygnage olyuer anſwerd certes paynem enduced ſpeke ſuche wyſe hath wel taught gretter ne hyely myghteſt thou adiure wherfore knowe thou olyuer ſone reyner erle gene mooſe eſpecyal felowe rolland one twelue peres fayth ſayd fyerabras alwaye thought wel thou another thā thou ſaydeſt ſeen thyn ardaunt courage coude make aferde vpon fayt bataylle ſir oliuer 〈2 page missing〉 al blody whiche ſtroke olyuer moeued troubled fallen hys ſadel haue bowed afterward al broken hors began halte ſtroke whan comen hym ſelf wyth hye boy began 〈◊〉 ¶o lord god creatour euyl ſtroke haue receyued vyrgyn marye moder iheſus haue pyte ouer fyerſly cutteth ſwerde thys paynym yeuo grace may one haue hym made vpon hym ſelf ſygne croſſe fyerabras ſayd hym olyuer mahoun god wyth thys ſtroke maad aferde mayſt thou wel fele playe haue meruaylle though thou commaunde thy god euyl contente haue hurte ouer ſore y• ſtroke ¶neuertheles ſure thou ſhalt ſee ſōne goo reſte thou begynneſt chaū ge colour thy fyerce manere neuertheles contente thou retorne ſhall beſt tofore thou knowe fully ſtrengthe warne one thynge whan ſee blood yſſue body thenne doubleth myght ſtrengthe wote wel charles loueth moche whan ſendeth yf lodged fayre bedde whyte ſhetes thou haddeſt moche better whan olyuer herde hym ſo ſays replenyſſhed feruent courage began lyfte vp hys heed ſayd paynym dyſmeſured al day thou vannteſt brynge thende dayes praye god almyghty wyl reioye courage kepe wel deffye haue ouer long pleted vpon theſe wordes rāne gydre ſmytyng meruayllouſly eche vpon helmes ſuche wyſe boucle naylles crochettes precious ſtones orfaueryes floures wen broken flowen grounde fyre yſſued oute largely makyng grete bruyt ſwerdes vpon harnoys whyle charles grete medytacyon thought quarele olyuer trewe iuſte god ought preſerue hym whan thought olyuer myght deye inpacyent perfayte fayth ſayd ¶o gloryous god whome take payne praye conſerue oliuer ſlayn ne taken ſwere ſoule fader yf ſlayn thys paynym neuer fraūce ony chirche ſhal clerke ne preeſt reueſted ne enhabyted ſhal brēne monaſteryes chyrches oulters crucyfyxes ala ſayd duc naymes syr kyng leue theſe wordes vayne ydle praye god olyuer ayde hys holy mercy al thys whyle perſeuerd ij champyons fyghtyng ſmytyng eche ſuche maner fyerabras wyth hys ſwerde brake cercle olyuers helme made hym falle hys vyſage hys hors ſlayn yf lepte ſyde olyuer hurte hys body ſpecyally breſte thenne loſte ſoo moche hys blood moche feble whyche merueylle ſeen reſyſted ageynſt mooſt terryble man euer borne moder ¶how olyuer made prayer god whan felte hym hurte capitulo xj olyuer noble erle beyng malancolye grete woundes hys body took recomforte ſayeng manere gloryous god cauſe begynnyng al aboue vnder fyrmamente owne playſer fourmed fyrſt fader adam hys companye gaueſt vnto hym eue whome al humayn generacyon conceyued gyuyng lycence ete al maner fruytes reſerued onely one whyche eue moeuyng ſerpent cauſed adam ete wherfore loſte paradys ſeduetyon fendes helle many haue ben deceyued dampned wherof ye pyte perdycyon world came take fleſſhe humayn wombe gloryous vyrgyn marye thannuncyacion holy aungel gabryel borne pleaſed anone thre kynges camen adoure make obeyſſaunce wyth golde encence myrre made preſentes herodes made ſlayne many chyldren whiche ioye permanable whan ye age determyned ye went world prechyng frendes thenne afterward thenuyous iewes ye hanged croſſe whiche ſo hangyng longyus knyght induction iewes percyd ſyde whā hyleued weſſhe hys eyen precious blode recouerd ſyȝt fayre clere cryed mercy wherby ſaued frēdes ye layed holy ſepulture thyrd day aroos took ageyn lyf deſcended helle took adam eue al worthy haue paradys day meruayllous aſcencyon ye aſcended heuen preſc̄ce al •• ſtles thus god maker thys trouthe byleue verayly fermly ye comforte ageynſt thys myſcrraunte may vaynquyſſhe hym ſuche wyſe may ſaued ſaid bleſſyd hym ſwerde makyng ſygne y• croſſe name god holy trynyte ſmote hors vpon hope helpe god fyerabras ſayd hym lawhyng olyuer fayre frende praye thou hyde frome oryſō thou haſt ſaid god termagaūt wold gladly wold god heuen ſayd olyuer thou ſuche grace thou ſholdeſt byleue alſo fermly doo aſſure ſhold loue thenne moche doo roulland ¶and fyerabras anſuerd hym god mahoun termagaunt thou ſpekeſt moche grete folye ¶how grete bataylle olyuer conquerd bawme dranke therof hys eaſe fyl therthe whan hys hors ſlayn capitulo xij fyerabras beyng wroth wordes oliuer grete ire ſayd hym kepe wel fro deffye redy ſayd olyuer god commaunde ſo thenne recountred gyder ſo ſharply ſo hard ſtrokes gaf fyre myȝt haboundantlye ſeen ſprynge oute theyr harnoys theyr horſes bowed vnder hem erthe trembled vruyt medowe vnder mormyonde fyerabras took hys ſwerde hys honde ſmote olyuer euyl hurt breſte vnder pappe ſtroke eyen torned hys heed hys face alle chaunged thenne ageyn cryed god virgyn marie wold ſaue ſoule fyerabras grete cartoſye ſayd hym olyuer vnder ſtonde deſcende doun ſurely goo take bawme drynke thyn eaſe anone thou ſhalt al guaryſſhed hole thenne mayſt thou better deffende ageynſt thou ſhalte recoure newe ſtrengthe olyuer noothynge coude though ſhold dye wold trewe fightyng wold haue anone came one ageynſt ſmyten ſuche wyſe fyerabras hurte daungerouſly olyuers ſwerde entred thye halfe foot depe blood yſſued oute alle graſſe reed whan ſawe hym ſo hurte dranke hys bawme anone al hool wherof olyuer moche ſorouful cauſe therof coude make none ende thys paynym frenſſhe men ſaw made god prayer deuontly wolde conſerue day olyuer eſpecyal charlemayn whiche emong al loued hym moaſt entyerly whan olyuer ſawe paynym al hole bawme ſo comforted ayde god came hym ſmote hym vpon helme ſoo harde ſtroke deſcended vpon ſadel cutte corde whyche barylles boū den faſtned hors fyerabras aferde ſtroke made lytel courſe playſyr god thenne olyuer paynym toke ony hede bowed grounde took vp barylles dranke hys eaſe largely anon al hole reconfermed newe ſtrengthe thought yf aduenture fyerabras hurte hym myght ageyn haue hys baryllys thende myght euyl happe come hym wherfore beyng nyghe vnto grete ryuer took barylles threwe therin whyche anone ſon • en redde alle feſtes ſaynt iohan theſe ij barylles ben ſhewed aboue water euydently whan fyerabras ſawe battlles loſte moſt angre oute hys mynde grete reproche ſayd olyuer euyl man thou arte thou haſt loſte barylles whyche worth al golde world promyſe euen ſhal ben dere ſolde ſhall ceſſe tyl haue ſmyton thy heed thys ſayeng came ayenſt hym olyuer doubteth hym ſoo moche dyd tofore eſchewed hym put hym defence wyth ſhelde auoyde ſtroke neuertheles fyerabras ſmote hym ſo hard yt hys helme deſmaylled broken hurte ſtroke deſcended ſo inpytuouſly y• cutte aſondre necke oliuers hors fyl groūde thēne olyuer fote grete myracle hors fyerabras maad ſemblaūte renne vpon hym ben taught lyke haue ſayd byfore helde hym ſtylle aboue hys propre cuſtome ¶how fyerabras olyuer foughten gyder afo • e merueyllouſly prayer charles maad olyuer capitulo xiij moche ſorouful frenſſhe men whan ſawe olyuer fote wold haue armed hem ſocoure hym charles wold conſente mayntene hys honour hys trouthe ¶and thenne kyng charles kneled doun therthe maad prayer god wolde comforte olyuer whyche thus dyſpourueyed hors whan olyuer ſawe hym ſelf fote moche ſorouful came foure paas nyghe vnto fyerabras ſayd hym kyng alexandrye thou haſt borne foule day ageynſt mornyng thou haſt ſo moche preyſed thy ſelf thou haſt ſayd yf v knyghtes came ageynſt thou woldeſt abyde conquere thou knoweſt kyng ſleeth hors ought haue parte therytage fyerabras anſuerd knowe wel thou ſayeſt trouthe dyd wyth wylle neuertheles thende thou euyl contente wyth ſhal deſcende doun hors ſhal gyue hors pomeld promyſe thou ſhalt well horſed knowe thou neuer lyf ſo abaſſhed whan ſawe erthe ſtrangled neuer put man erthe thys hors preſent anone hym ſlayn dede olyuer anſuerd promyſe ſhal neuer take thyn hors yf firſt conquered iuſtly wonne wherupon fyerabras ſoo moche noble valyaunce olyuer ſayd certeyn nobleſſe knowe wyl neuer dyd mā ſprange hors ſtode foote contente fyght ayenſt hym foote cauſe hors hys owne ſayd fyerabras moche heyer olyuer one accorde iuſted afoote one ayenſt ſo meruayllouſly wonder bothe tweyne remayned felde ſwoune trauaylle toke thus contynuēg bataylle coude take none ende ſpaken many reproches deſpytrous wordes one theym vnto kyng charles ſeyng al thys grete pyte olyuer thenne erle reyner fader olyuer whyche moche ſorouful came kneled foot charles ſayd noble emperour thonour god take remors ſone whome ſee lykly anone dye atte leſte make prayer iheſus maker ayde hym may ſee hym nyghe helthe ¶incontynent charles ſeyng thys ſayd lord god yf ye ſuffre olyuer ouercome ryght thys tyme loſte defyled make auowe al cryſtyante ſhal deſtroyed ſhal leue fraunte chirche ne monaſterye ymage ne aulter kneled doun bothe knee groūde prayed manere creatour whyche ſauacyon borne gloryous vyrgyn marie bethleem wel byleue glorious byrth al world enlumyned whiche abode thys world ful xxxij yere made atte begynnyng adam eue ben comen paradys terreſtre place moche delectable alle f •• ytes abandoned except one onely whyche knowyng good euyl pleſed ordeyne whiche adam ete dyſobey ſaunt reparacion miſdede redeme hym fro eternal captyuyte v alſo ye contente take deth tree croſſe traycour iudas ſolde xxx pen friday ye payned handes foot mortally nay • led crowned moche ſharpe crowne thornes longyus ſmote ryght ſyde hert whiche blynde leyed hys eyen precyous blood ſawe moche clerely ye deſcended helle toke oute frendes ſythe arods fro doth lyf tofore al apoſtles ye aſcended heuen lefte lyeutenaūt ſaynt peter thappoſtle erthe ordeyneſt bapteſme regeneracyon v make v cryſten haue ſaluacyon lord alle thys tr •• byleue ſtedfirſtly ſo thys day thou ayde ſocour vnto olyuer preſerue hym ſlayn ne vaynauyſſhed ¶he thys ſayeng deuoute wordes hys ſecrete oratorye lord ſente hym aungel fro heuen whyche ſayd hym ¶o charles emperour nobleſſe knowe thou trouthe ſente god ſay thou doubte thynge olyuer wythout faylle ſhal wynne bataylle though late ſhal vaynquyſſhe paynym thys ſayd aūgel departed end charles thanked god deuoutelye hys gloryous dytacyon neuertheles many bataylles bytwene fyerabras olyuer maad grete menace grete furour wyllyng haue gyuen olyuer grete ſtroke oute meſure olyuer whyche ſawe ſtroke comyng deuaunced hym ſuche wyſe gaf two euyl ſtrokes fyerabras wherof fyerabras paſſyng angry vpon olyuer olyuer hym ſo bothe ryȝt actyf neuer departe tyl one vaynquyſſhed deſtroyed tyme olyuer ſoo coueytous ſmytyng honde whiche helde hys ſwerde ſlepe ſwollen payne ſmytyng deſyryng ſmyte hys enemye vtteraunce hys ſuerde flewe ferre fro hym hande wherof ſore moeued abaſſhed meruaylle moche courageouſly rāne take vp ſwerde layed hys ſhelde hys hede preſerue wythſtōdyng paynym ſmote hym twyes ſo myghtyly brake hys ſhelde dyuers place hys hauberke ſo ſore aſtonyed tyme doubted ſoo moche paynym durſt take hys ſwerde moche ſodeynlye frenſſhe men ſawe ſo olyuer dyſponrueyed ſwerde armed anone purpoos renne vpon ſaraſyn ſocour olyuer charles wold conſente ony man ſhold goo ſayeng god almyghty ſaue mayntene hym hys good ryght yf gaynſayed thā xiiij thouſand men thenne redy haue reſcowed hym wythſtondyng al thys paynym dyd laughe ſaid olyuer trouthe olyuer haue opteyned vpon lytel myn entente wherfore darſt y• take thy ſwerde knowe wel thou art ynough vaynquyſſhed ſythe thou art ſo aferde thou darſt ſtoupe treſour world wel contēte apoynte wyth thou renye fayth thou holdeſt bapteſme thou haſt receyued god thou byleueſt whome thou haſt al thys payne byleue mahoun god ful bounte ſhal ſuffre lyue ouer ſhal contente gyue ſiſter wy • thou ſhalte rychely maryed hyr name florypes fayreſt moder borne ſhal conquere fraunce thys yere paſte one royames ſhal crowne kyng olyuer anſuerd hym paynym thou ſpekeſt grete folye god forbede euer ſhold entencion forſake god whyche hath created fourmed holy ſacrements haue eſtablyſſhed fo • ſauacyon byleue mahoun thy goddes ful abuſyon whiche haue neyther ſtrengthe ne vertue cauſe dampnacyon fyerabras ſayd hym mahoun god thou art alwaye moche obſtynat ne payn ne torment thou wylt denye thy fayth one thynge grete thou mayſt wel auaūte neuer perſone ſo trauailled ne greued ¶thou oughteſt wel prayſed contente thou take thy ſwerde hardyly ſurely withoute competent wepen thou mayſt preuaylle ne thā woman olyuer anſwerd paynym ſay contrarye thou offreſt ſeruyce bounte valewe x thouſand marke golde wyl take ne deye therfore yf recouerd ſwerde thy curtoſye happed thou vnder puyſſaunce thou thenne demaundeſt amytye frendſhyp thenne put deth ſhold vylete reproche thys tyme lyf deth wylle god haue gyuen ſelf ouer yf may wynne ſwerde thou ſhalt bye dere deye thynge ſhal thou haue ¶by fayth ſayd fyerabras thou art moche ſurquydrous gloryous wherfore thou ſure ſhortely thou ſhalt confuſed deſcomfyte matte ¶how thys bataylle fyerabras vaynquyſſhed olyuer recouerd one ſwerdes fyerabras capitulo xiiij whan fyerabras herde oliuer ſo fyers fayt courage grete meruaylle wold haue hys ſwerde yf myght iuſte warre conquere wherfore paynym dyſmeſurably came ageynſt hym helde hys hande plorance hys ſwerde thenne meruayle though olyuer aferde abyde hys enemye beyng dyſpourueyed ſwerde ſhelde broken two partyes playſed god loked beſyde hym ſawe hors fyerabras arſon ſadel ij ſwerdes whych haue ſpoken afore anone olyuer ranne ryght quyckely took one ſwerdes whych named bapteſme whyche blade moche large ſhone meruayllouſly came ageynſt paynym put tofore parte hys ſhelde ſuche lefte whan nyghe hym began ſay kyng alexandrye tyme compte pourueyed ſwerde whych ſhal make wroth kepe wel haue deffyed thenne whan fyerabras ſawe herde hym ſo ſpeke anone began chaunge colour ſayd baptym good ſwerde haue kepte many day one beſte euer henge ſyde ony man lyuyng behelde olyuer ſayeng god mahoun knowe mā grete fyerſte wold thou woldeſt take thyn owne ſwerd late haue myn thenne late v fyght haue begonne hede ſayd olyuer ſhal neuer wylle tofore make ony pacte ſhall aſſaye approue thys ſwerde vpon thy perſone kepe wel fro ouer long haue ſermoned thys ſayeng thynges olyuer came lyon hungry ayenſt fyerabras ſmote hym fyrſt myȝt attayne hym hede recountred firſt ſhelde paynym whyche brake al fruſſhed euyl half flewe felde thenne fyerabras ſore aferde ſtroke aboue alle thys ſwerde wyth ſtroke entred nygh half foot within therthe thenne olyuer bleſſyd hym forged ſwerde ſo wel tempred many menace rygorous partye deſcouuerd theyr helmes whan olyuer ſawe paynym fyerabras vyſage fyers courageous ſayd lord god heuen maker heuen erthe thys paynym noble ful cruelte wold god charles hym power yf wold baptyſed rolland ſhold hys pryue felowes glorious vyrgyn marie moder god praye lord iheſu cryſte thy ſone gyue grace thys ſaraſyn may byleue criſten fayth hym may moche enhaunced fyerabras anſuerd thys manere olyuer leue ſuche wordes telle yf thou wylt fyght like thou haſt enterpryſed ye ſayd olyuer kepe wel fro ••• ffye ranne vpon hym olyuer ſmyton fyrſt vpon ſhelde ſuche fierſnes ſmote ſhelde pyeces nyghe hys fyſte meruaylle cut wherfore fyerabras ſayd put hym ſuche caas ſhold longe lyue thys world olyuer ſayd noo worde came ſwerde ayenſt paynym fyerabras moche furyouſly ¶thenne paynym ſawe y• ſtroke come threwe hys ſhelde ayenſt olyuer wherfore anone quartred ſo aſtoned eyen heed al troubled payne fyre ſeen ſprynge oute ſwerdes ſheldes moche habundantlye thus ſmytyng fyerabras ſayd manere houre come thou ſhalt neuer haue ayde thy god iheſus whome thou byleueſt anone thou ſhalt deed ſythe thou feleſt thy ſelf ouercomen olyuer anone anſuerd iheſus wel myghty ſhewe hys puyſſaunce anone thou ſhalt knowe mahoun ne termagaunte ſhal mowe ayde ne ſo myghty thou ſhalte deed ſhal wel gyue knowleche herupon came one vpon olyuer ſmyton helm al vnto fleſſhe ſuche wyſe al ſwerde araught ſhare paſſed thorugh thenne ſayd olyuer ſuere god haue wel araught ſmyton neuer ſhal charles ne rolland ſee thou wel ſure olyuer anſuerd fyerabras aleyandrye thou ſo proude departe fro ſhal rendre dede vaynquyſſhed god graunte whyche haue alwaye deſyred therupon eche ſmote ſo merueyllouſly bodyes bothe ſwette anguyſſhe payne fyerabras ſmote olyuer vpon helme ſoo harde ſtoke came fleſſh yf god wrought ſlayn tyme wherfore olyuer man enraged came ayenſt paynym ſaraſyn lyfte hyghe hys ſhelde ſo al dyſcouerd vnder arme hys flanke vnarmed olyuer wyſe took good hede came lyghtly ſmote fyerabras hys flāke ſo myghtyly contynued ſuche wyſe threſted ſwerde one hys flankes wel depe hys ſwerde hym ſelf place alle bybled blood thus fyerabras hurte ſuche manere almooſt hys lowellys yſſued oute bely thenne ſtroke olyuer employed al ſtrengthe make ende bataylle ſo longe foughten ¶how fyerabras beyng vaynquyſſhed byleued god borne olyuer olyuer aſſaylled ſaraſyns tormented capitulo xv paynym ſmyton hurte mortally haue ſayd ſeyng myght nomore teſyſte ayenſt olyuer vertu god enlumyned ſuche wyſe knowleche errour paynyms lyfte vp hys eyen vnto heuen began eſcrye holy trynyte grace holy ghoſt loked olyuer ſayd hym noble olyuer valyaunt knyght thonour god whome thou byleueſt whome conſente crye mercy requyre dye tyl baptyſed yelden vaynquyſſhed vnto charles emperour whyche ſo moche redoubted ſhal byleue cryſten fayth ſhal yelde relyques whyche ye aſſemblyd haue taken ſoo moche payne ſwere yf thy defaute dye ſaraſyn make culpable dampnacyon yf thou take thy garde ſhal loſe blood thou ſhalt ſee deye tofore thyn eyen wherfore honour god haue pyte olyuer ſo moche compaſſyon hym hys ſoor ſore wepte layed hym ſhadowe vnder tree boūde mortal woūdes ſuche wyſe ſtaunched hys bledyng paynym prayed hym myght pleſe hym bere hym awaye hym ſelf myght goo whan olyuer ſawe ſo heuy ſayd hym poſſyble bere hym fyerabras enforced hym ſelf moche came nyghe hym noble redoubted erle olyuer honour god lede charles dede nyghe myn ende al body bledeth take hors mounte ſhewn come nyghe thou may yf may lye thwart tofore vpon ſadel thou mayſt lede take ſwerde thy ſyde ¶now haſt thou foure moche worthe hye depeſſhe thys day mornyng lefte wode thou ſeeſt fyfty thouſand men whyche al ſubgettes commanded none ſhold moeue tyl retorned fro bataylle whan olyuer vnderſtood hym al afrayed abaſſhed fere wythſtondyng ſayd syr kyng ſythe pleſe contente took hym thwart hors ſayd went forth waye grete ſorowe ſodeynly departed wode ſubgettes fyerabras moche fyers paynym named bruyllant mommere hym sortybrant nonymbres kynge mantryble hym maradas pynan tenebras wel fyfty thouſand ſaraſyns whan olyuer ſawe theym come ſmote hors wyth ſpores charge ſo heuy myȝt goo ſo faſte enemyes came hym whan frenſſhe men ſawe paynyms come ſo grete nombre anon lyghtely armed emonge rolland gherard mondydyer guyllam ſcot naymes bauyere ogier rychard normādye guy bourgoyn geffroy lantiguy baſyn due thyery ardeyne aubert ſemblably reyner gene fader olyuer faylled olyuer ſaw alonge medowe ſawe come fore thother brullāt mōmyere rode hors ſwyft grehounde made grete bruyt emonge ſemed thonder tempeſte bare hys honde faus dart grete lede ſtele ſquare ſharpe whyche alle enuenymed wyth blood crapauſd ryght daungerous whan olyuer ſawe hym al amo • ued abaſſhed ſayd fyerabras thys manere sir kyng ye muſt nedes deſcente may ferther conduyte • ou wherfore meruayll • uſly ſory dyſplayſaunt knowe muſt nedes oppreſſyd ye ſee wel yf may attayne ſhal • ut deth charles ſhal neuer ſee whyche ſhall hym grete dyſcomforte thenne anone fyerabras cryed hye veys noble olyuer wyl ye leue ye haue conquerd yeuen yelden ſhal reputed nobleſſe determyned whan youres ye forſake ala poure ſorouful caytyf yf deye paynym ſhal come virgyn marie moder god haue pyte vnworthy retorne ſayd olyuer conquerd haue promyſed ſhal baptyſed yf thou leue thou oughteſt lytel preyſed olyuer anſuerd fyerabras thou ſpekeſt knyght auowe god courte heuen ſhal leue ſhal take bataylle honde ſhal deffende longe ſhal lyue thou mayſt wel truſte therto vpon took hauberk ſaraſyn wyth ſuche myȝt haue armed hym preſtly abylled hym put heed hatte fyn ſtele helde hys ſwerde drawen named haultelere wyth whiche coude wel helpe hym hereupon came anone brullant wyth faus darte atteyned olyuer breſte gaf hym euyl ſtroke ſo dart brake thēne ſaid fyerabras syr olyuer ye haue doon ynough ye hurte late deſcende doun laye parte waye thende defoulled theſe ſaraſyns ne taken deſtroyed therof olyuer grete compaſſyon layed fyerabras ſhadowe pynapple tree forre waye whan wold haue fledde ſawe aboute hym wel x thou ſand ſaraſyns ſayd ala god iheſus creatour thou knoweſt myn entencyon requyre gyue grace deye thys tyme preſent vnto tyme thexaltacion thy fayth may wyth rolland felawe name iheſus drewe haulte clere came waye firſt recoūtred ſone gretteſt lord gaf hym ſuche ſtroke clefte hym breſte fyl doun dede olyuer abylle delyuer took fro hym hys ſhelde whyche al newe bataylle tofore maad loſte hys alſo ſpere lete hys hors renne emonge myſcreauntes atteyned fyrſt ſtroke clorgys ſmote hym vnto hert retornyng ſlewe thre ſaraſyns rāne tofore hym ſheep tofore wulf whiche hongry thenne came hym mara ba turgys sortybrant conymbres kyng margaris cryed hye voys gydre mahoun god thou frēſſhe man thou ſhalt eſcape v kepe wel v thou ſhalt deye thenne cam olyuer emonge enemyes ſmote ſlewe al ſydes ſareſyns ſmote hym ſuche wyſe grete meruaylle ſlayne ouercomen force ſhotte ſtrokes hys hors ſlayn vnder hym beyng erthe ſone myght aroos beyng afoot ſette ſhelde tofore hym whyche goten helde faſt haultclore whyche alle hys comforte ſocoure hym alwaye whome raught fyl doun ſlayn redde ony book euer ony man ſo hurt bare hym ſo wel dyd ſo grete portemente armes ¶how olyuer taken blynfeld pyteouſly myght ſocoured frenſſhe men capitulo xvij olyuer allone fote emong ſaraſyns ageynſt whome made grete reſyſtence meruayllous thynge poſſyble myght eſcape fro theyr handes wyth glayues ſwerdes faus dartes yron preſſyd hym ſo fore hys ſhelde perced moo xxx place whan hys hawberk broken perced wyth foure ſharpe dartes perced wounded hym body meruaillouſly wherfore veray force febleſſe fyl erthe took hym moche outerageouſly blynfelde hys eyen bonde hym ſtraytely ſoo myȝt ſee ne wyſt ſette hym vpon good hors bonde hym ſurely whan thys valyaunt olyuer thus dyſpourueyed fro al helpe fro al ſyȝt fro al hope fro al comforte good wete grete deſplayſaunce knewe wold doo wyth hym thenne wyth hye voys compaſſyon hert ſayd charlemayn kyng nobleſſe emperour valure art thou knoweſt thou ſeeſt thou remembreſt noble felawe rolland thou art ſlepe deef may none cryſten remembreth theſe ſuche complayntes makyng kyng maradas ſayd hym frenſſhe man ſomeuer thou thou ſpekeſt folye ſhal ete tyl thou hanged theſe ſaraſyns ranne wyth olyuer • yen blynfelde hys hondes ſtraytly bounden garde four fals tyrant thēne vpon thys eſpecyal came rolland thyerry al peres charles hym ſelf alſo thys ouer late ſaue olyuer wyth grete cryes cryed god al ſayntes heuen wyth grete ire rolland ſmote corſuble breſt gherard mondydyer came ayenſt turgys ogyer ſmote athena rychad amancdys guy bourgoyne atteyned brullant none peres fraunce ouer thre hys man made ſo grete dyſcomfyte ſaraſyns al empeſſhed holde gyders goo theyr waye paynyms conduyted olyuer wente alwaye forth thys bataylle ſlayn guyllam gaultier ynow valyaunte peple many moyen people laye grounde gherard de mondydier ſone duke thyerey geffroy langeuyn bonde dylygently theyr horſes rode aweye wyth haſtely whan charles ſawe theym thus fadde angre loſte almooſt hys wytte wyth hyghe voys cryed ſaue kepe ſocoure baron knyȝtes deſloyal ye ſlowe yf lede awaye baron neuer ſhal ye fare wel whan frenſſhe men herde charles thus moeued enraged ſmote theyr horſes wyth theyr ſports wente doun mountayn rolland fyrſt helde hys ſwerde durandall drawen tauenge hym fyerſly hym atteyned ſure paſſe deth al enraged cauſe ledde aweye felowe olyuer ſmote paynym clefte hym myddle hys body tyme rolland bare hym myghtely cauſe multytude paynyms myght paſſe forth ſocoure baron pryſonners chaced v myle ferre coude approche thenne many good knyghtes deed morfounded wery wythſtondyng rolland ſware wold neuer retorne tyl baron fraunce taken fro handes theyr enemyes myght nyght came wyſt neuer whyther goo ſaraſyns tofore went fleyng alwaye theyr playſyr ¶thys ſeyng charles wyſt ſhold doo ne ſay doubted paynyms made watche ryere garde cloſe ¶and therfore force muſt leue felde ryȝt grete dyſplayſyr anguyſſhe ſo al retorned ¶the ſecond partye ſecond book conteyneth xvij chapytres ſpeketh tormente baron fraunce taken ſpaken ballant thadmyral ſpayne ¶how fyerabras foūden charles baptyſed heled wounde capitulo primo charles knew myght haue ageyn olyuer ne pryſoners force hym retorne wyth hys people nyght thēne greuous alſo retornyng fonde fyerabras vnder tre languyſſhyng ye kyng ſaid vnhappy paynym ouȝt wel hate men pryſonners boſte thou haſt take fro oliuer one beſt byloued emonge al thumayn creature hym y• hath ſynguler mayntene good name ende ſtede ioye thou yeldeſt ſorowe whan fyerabras vnderſtode hym ſore ſyghed ſayd ryche emperour noble mooſt myghty humayn lygnage thonour god crye mercy pardone trouthe olyuer hath conquerd ſhal hyde haue promyſed hym ſhal cryſtned haue left forſaken al goddes yelde iheſus creatour world requyre yet may baptyſed yf heled woundes ſhal enhaūce power cryſten fayth many ſaraſyns ſhal maad cryſten moyan holy ſepulcre holy reliques ſhal delyuerd whome ye take grete payne trauaylle alſo make oth god byleue heuy ſory olyuer noble knyȝt whiche taken pryſonner body whyche morrally wounded grace god ſhal haue hym one wherfore conclude cryſtened yf deye ſaraſyn ſhal reproche ¶and vpon thys charles whyche grete compaſſyon hym made hym borne hys ledgyng baron whan ſaw hym ſo hugely mēbred al abaſſhed gretenes largenes whan v • armed one ſemelyeſt men euer ¶and al frenſſhe men gaf grete loss honour olyuer foughten ouercomen ſuche man vnclothed partye hys woundes opened began blede wherof hys hert faylled fyl doun ſwoune rolland anone lyfte hym vp al haſte made redy fonte ſente thachebyſſhop turpyn naymes moche ioyous paynym ſhold cryſtend bapteſme redy godfaders gaf hym another name named floren longe lyued called fyerabras thenne layed bedde honourable laſte ende hys dayes ſaynt god ſhewed hym myracles called saynt floren roye thenne anone charles made hym vyſyted medycynes ſurgyens wel expert ſerche den al woundes god wolde fonde none bowellys ētamed ne hurt wherfore lech ſure delyuer hym al hole wythin ij monethes next comyng makyng vyſytacion emperour charles preſent ſayd fyerabras yf olyuer baron preſent tofore ſhold wel contente charles thenne al pencyf heuy moche thynkyng vpon hys baron pryſoners maad ſemblaunte ¶how olyuer felowes preſented ballant thadmyral cruelly paſſyoned pryſon capitulo ij ſaraſyns baron fraūce tofore named pryſoners taryed ranne tyl came ryche cytee named agrymore entre ſayd cyte ſowned blewe vp trumpes makyng grete bruyt whan ballant thadmyral fader fyerabras ſawe came vnto fonde brullant mōmyer whome ſayd brullant frende •• lle v tydynges ye haue borne warre affayres haue ye taken charles emperour whyche ſo moche redoubted peres fraunce dyſcomfyted brullant ſayd hym ſyr admyral tydynges brynge alle otherwyſe laſſe valewe ye ſay charles kyng haue almooſt defeated dyſcomfyted hys puyſſaunce meruayllous thynge fyerabras ſone hym vaynquyſſhed one baron made cryſten taken vaynquyſſhed dyſcomfyted loyal batayl without doyng ony treaſon whan thadmyral vnderſtode fyl therthe al traunſe came ageyn hys mynde grete whyle ſowwe hys ſone whan releued cryed wyth hye voys dolaunt vnhappy ha poure caytyf ſhal bycome fyerabras ryght dere ſone heyer whyther art thou gone fro whens cometh thys treſpaas wherfore thou taken whyche neuer bataylle wery ne reproche ¶o euyl tydynges brought yf cryſten ſory lyueth moche leuer dyſmembred put deth thenne man feble ſorowe fyl doun grounde cryed brullant mommyere betyd noble kyng cordube neuewe bruchart ſythe ſone fyerabras ledar captayn yf trewe loſt ſhal ſmyte oute brayne mahōmet god whiche hath promyſed ſo moche good whome haue gyuen ſelf yolden thus ſayeng alle rage tormented hym ſelf greuouſly vpon grounde whan thadmyral lytel coled hys grete yre demaunded brullant whiche knyȝt hath vaynquyſſhed fyerabras ſone brullāt anſwerd syr admyrall ſone hath conquerd yonde knyght ſhewyng olyuer whiche ſo fayr wel formed membred emonge al eyen bended anone ſayd thadmyral ſpayn hye brynge hym ſhal neuer ete tyl 〈…〉 membred whan frenſſh men vnderſtode wold put olyuer deth whiche al theyr comforte begonne greuouſly olyuer whiche vnderſtode ſawe waylle recomforted ſayeng ſuche manere ſaraſyns wyſt ſayd lordes brethern ye knowe neceſſite yf thadmyral myȝt know peres fraūce lyues ſhal ſone termyned thyng ſhal take ryte v ſhal deye ſhamefully wherfor praye al ſay ſhal begynne whome alle frenſſhe men pryſōners dyd conſente wold ſay lyke counceylled thadmyral comanded come tofore hym paynyms vnarmed bonde faſt theyr hondes blynfelde theyr eyen wherof moche greued daungerouſly hurt anon thadmyral furiouſly demaūded olyuer y• frenſſh mā beware y• lye ſay trouthe thou arte named hyde olyuer anſuerd ſayd ſyr named engynes ſone vnto yeman poure lygnage borne lorayne cam tyme courte charles emperour whiche gaf armes adoubed knyght alſo felawes ye ſee tofore ben poure knyghtes aduenturous haue enterpryſed payne ſerue kyng bycauſe yt ſeruyce myȝt auaunced haue ſōme good guerdon rewarde mahoun ſayd thadmyral wel deceyued ſuppoſed god fyue valyaunteſt erles fraunce greteſt thought kayes fraunce moyen theſe baron anone called barba • chamberlayn ſayd hym anone depeſſhe take theſe frenſſhe men deſpoyle bynde harde pyler brynge dartes wel ſharped wyth yron ſhal ſhote ſmyte hem playſyr thēne aroos brullant ſayd ſyr admyral praye thys tyme ye enterpryſe ſhal wel doo ye ſee wel euentyde ouer late iuſtyce ſo ye myght blamed ſeen ſeygnorye ne lordes preſent wherfore praye thys tyme ye thyng tyl morowe atte houre eche man knowe iugemēt ſhal better approued knowe wel haue deſerued wel euydently ſyde yf charles emperour wold yelde ageyn fyerabras ſone wyth good wylle ye myght ſemblably remyſe hym theſe frēſſh men ye haue loue ſayd thadmyral contente ſente brutamont whych kepar pryſon gaf hym grete charge kepe frenſſhe men wel f •• ſette ſuche place lerne haue wrought folyly come hys kepyng ¶of pryſon wherein frenſſhe men lodged vyſyted fayre florypes doughter admyral beaulte hyr capitulo iij ballant thadmyral spayne commaunded frenſſhe men ſette greuous pryſon brutamont geayler made olyuer felawes auale doun pryſon moche daungerous whyche ſo depe ſtrayt groūde lyȝt myght ſeen put nouryſſhed ſerpentes crapauldes beeſtes venemous deteſtable whyche place al ſtenche compryſed paſſed ſtreme ſalte ſee whiche hys entree wythout conduyt whiche water myght one paſſe whan tyde paſſed kepar pryſon went blynfeld ſhet dore aboue beyng fylthe ſtenche anon water came ſo habūdantly poure frēſſh men water vnto ſholdres thenne woūdes olyuer began ſmerte cauſe ſalte water perced hys hert ye may wel thynke payne grete eſpecyal olyuer hurt mortally many place grete neceſſyte remedye place al paynes renewed woundes opened anon felte hym bayned ſalte water fyl doun ſwoune dede tyme ne gherard de mondydyer ſuſteyned hym ye may demaūde drowned ſeeyng water grewe alwaye ye ſhal vnderſtonde pryſon ¶madame ſaid porter frēſſh men longyng charles kyng whiche neuer ceſſe deſtroye lawe ſhe peple repreue creaūce ſette nought goddes haue ben aydyng ſlee fyerabras broder emong ther one grete valure whyche one beſt made men euer knowen hath ben ſo myghty conquerd loyal batayl fyerabras anone floryres enuye hym ſpeke ſayd brutamōt wyl ſpeke hem come opene pryſon wyl knowe theyr fayt brutamont anſwerd ſayd madame ye ſhal pardonne ye may ſee cauſe fylthe dyſhoneſte place apperteyneth ſyde fader hath deffended noo perſone ſhal approche pryſon remembre wel oftymes woman haue knowen ſomme ſhamed deceyued whan floripes vnderſtood ſhe angre almooſt fro hyr ſelf ſayd hym euyl glouton deſpytous oughteſt thou yeue ſuche langage promyſe ſhal make payed ſhortly called hyr chamberlayn whyche gaf hyr ſtaffe ſhe made ſemblaunte opene pryſon brutamont gaynſayed ſodeynly ſhe ſeyng porter wythſtonde hyr gaf hym ſuche ſtroke vyſage y• ſhe made hys eyen flee oute hys heed fyl doun ſhe ſhewe hym threwe hym wythout knowyng ſaraſyns pryſon frenſſhe men wherof ſore aferde abaſſhed whan herd hym wenyng deuyl wold haue tempted deceyued thenne anone florypes dyd doo lyght torche dyd open pryſon put lyght tofore hyr ſee pryſonners cam nyghe pyler ſayd ¶o • ye lordes telle ye ar ye named hyde ye thyng fro olyuer anſuerd ſaid fayr lady ben fraunce men charle mayns haue ben brouȝt hyther thadmyral hath comaunded v thys cruel priſon moche better v dyd v dyſmembred dye tabyde place curtoys florypes withſtondyng y• ſhe cryſtened ſo grete nobleſſe ſo grete compaſſyon ſaid promyſe ſhal put pryſon ſo ye promette ſwere ye ſhal helpe ſhal ſay olyuer anſuerd therof madame aſſure ye ſhal fynde v ſuche effecte ye ſhal deſyre faythful trewe neuer ne neuer ſhal ye ſure ſhall neuer fayle longe ſhall haue lyf bodyes ſe y• furnyſſhed armes aboue meddle wyth ſaraſyns ſhal make grete dyſcomfyte vaſſal ſayd doughter ye may auaunte ouer moche yet ye wel ferre oute yet menace ye ben theyr lyberte better man wyſely ſtylle folyſſhly ſpeke gherard ſayd lady damoyſel ſhal ſaye one worde deteyned ſtrongely empeſſhed ſingeth gladly forgete payne melancolye floripes byhelde gherard curtoys whyche excuſed olyuer whyche ſpake ouer hardyly thys grete meruaylle ioye olyuer whan lady ſaid hym ſhold put oute pryſon hym thought thenne armed free wylle lady ſayd gherad ¶in trouthe ſyr ye wel ſay excuſe felowe redyly byleue veryly ye wel playe maydens eage ſōme chambre vnder curteynes dyſporte loue trowe ye knowe maner guillam ſcot anſwerd ſayd ſowle madame ye ſay ſoth hym ye haue wel deuyned fro hen vnto iijc myle ye ſhal fynde hys pere ¶how frenſſhe men put outo pryſon vyſyted noble mayde floripes beaulte hyr chambre capitulo iiij whan fayr florypes ſpoken hir playſyr wyth baron pryſonners ſhe called hir chamberlayn made hym brynge corde ſtaffe bounden ouerthwart lete doun whan frenſſhe men ſawe made fyrſt olyuer goo vp lady hyr chamberleyn drewe hym vp grete force wente vp lyghtly ynough ſhe ledde wodes montaynes byrdes beeſtes fyſſhe paynted fygures lykeneſſe meruayllous facyon ſōme ſcryptures ſone mathuſſale dyd make thys chambre ſtood vpon blacke roche al enuyronned wyth ſee one quarter gardyn pretoyre meruaylouſly fayr wherin floures ne fruytes faylled neuer al maladyes ſekeneſſes ſauf onely maladye ot deth founden comforte good helpe within grewe mandegloyre fayr floripes gellerye theſe ladyes clarmondyne florette florymonde many fayr vyrgynes hir maiſtreſſe named maragonde ſayd florypes madame knowe wel theſe frenſſhe men yonder goodly man ye ſee olyuer whyche ſone reyner gene broder audeyne one fayreſt borne woman thys hath vaynquyſſhed fyerabras thy broder gherard mondidier oftymes hath prayſed honoured willyam ſcot camuſe whyche hyndmeſt geffroy langeuyn praye god mahomet curſe yf euer ete drynke tyl haue tolde fader lord thadmyrall floripes anone chaunged al colour whan ſhe herde theſe wordes moche ſecretly ſhe reteyned hyr ire ayenſt hyr called thys woman hir wyndowe gaf hyr ſo grete ſtroke ſhe fyl grounde called varlet whyche cam hyr preſtly threwe woman ſee florypes redoubted moche hyr fader malyce whan thys olde woman tombled ſee florypes ſayd hyr ¶now goo thou olde deſpytous wretche thou haſt thy guerdon ſure frenſſhe men ben ne ſhal neuer en combred ne daunger herof baron made grete ioye thenne floripes noble lady came vnto frenſſhe men kyſſed ſwetely whan ſhe ſawe oliuer whyche al blody knewe wel hurte ſhe ſayd hym syr olyuer ne doubte ye ſhal rendre anone al hole good helthe wente mandegboyre took lytel anone oliuer vſed al hele reduced good helthe baron beyng noble chambre anone good fyre ſette table wel pourueyed al good vytaylle delycyous mete whyche grete nede bycauſe grete hungre thenne endured mete buynes chauffed thenne bayned refayted theyr eaſe comyng theyr baynes wel adoubed wyth mantel ryche ſylke golde broundred thēne floripes ſayd lordes burons ye knowe wel haue put ſelf grete daunger brynge oute pryſon mortal ye ſurete ferre man hath herde v yf aduenture knowen ſhold torne v euyl doubte olyuer whyche preſent hath ouercomen brother whome naturelly ought repre • f knowe wel alle ye nothyng abaſſhed ye knowe wel rolland ¶on tyme whan rome ſawe hym ſythe tyme haue gyuen hym myn hert whan fader admyral deſtroyed rome lucafar bādas moche redoubted emonge paynyms ſayd guy bourgoyne iuſteden gyder ſayd guy men moche ioyous gyuen grete thankynges god good wylle thys fayre mayde gherard de mondydyer ſayd hyr madame ſwere yf armed halle emonge ſaraſyns ſhold make grete dyſcomfyture florypes wyſe ſayd wyth guy bourgoyne whome haue gyuen herte neuertheles conſyder wel chapytre grete werke compryſed whan fyrſt florypes curtoys paynym deſyre ſpeke wyth frenſſhe men alle toucheth wel deſyre wylle wymmen knowe newe thynges tydynges moche touched werke ſhe dyd ayenſt kepar pryſon taken oute werke man wel approued ben grete damage yf thoſe baron abyden pryſon fayth perſones doth grete alegement tormente ſayntes heuen theyr holy fayth haue obteyned heuen many terryen men victorye theyr enemyes wyth good ryght fyghteth fayth happe deteyned mercy god nyghe delyuer hym cauſe wherfore delyuerd cauſe ſauyng pryſoners whyche haue ſayd grete daunger ¶how kyng charles ſente ballant thadmyral ſeuen peres fraunce whyche wold haue goon capitulo v duc gene fader olyuer myȝt ſlepe ne ete ne drinke ſorowe ſone whan myght lenger endure came kyng charles ſayd hym syr emperour loue god haue pyte ye knowe ſorowe ought loſe olyuer ſone whome contynuell anguyſſhe yf haue none tydynges ſhal deye ij dayes melancolye force muſt put ſelf waye goo thyder whan charles vnderſtode hym moeued full compaſſyon melancolye reyner ſente rolland ſayd hym fayre neuewe rolland vnderſtonde morne mornyng thou muſt goo aygremore ſhalt ſay ballant thadmyral wythoute ony hydyng delyuer crowne iheſu cryſt relyques haue taken grete payne aſke hym baron holdeth pryſon yf wythſaye ſay hym ſhal hym druwen vylaynouſly hāge hym necke eye bounden theef whan ſaid rolland anſwerd syr kyng fayre vncle haue mercy wel ſure yf goo verayly ſhal neuer ſee ¶the duke naymes whyche ſayd ſyr emperour take hede ye doo rolland neuewe ye knowe valewe yf goo thyder ſhal neuer come ageyn aſſure ſayd charles ye ſhal goo wyth hym bere letter ſende thadmyral thys ſayd baſyn genewey came forth ſayd hym ſyr wyl ye thus aforeſayd came tofore charles ſyr naymes ſaid al emperour nobleſſe redoubted al place tobeye thy commaundement praye thou gyue v lycence congie departe yf ony perſone preſent al thexcerſyte hath mahommet god whome haue gyuen ſelf gyue euyl deth yf euer ete drynk tyl ſee thy hede flee fro thy ſholdres duc naymes anſuerd yf playſe god maker bleſſyd moder yu ſhalt haue made leſyng hym ſpake rychard duc normandye ſaid vnderſtonde ſyr admyral charles kyng lerde floryſſhed comandeth yt thou baptyſe tamende thy ryght euyl lyf thou ſende hym relyques thou haſt thy puyſſaunce alſo thou rendre hym hys knyghtes whyche thou holdeſt wythout reſon pryſoners yf thou thou haſt herde charles ſhal hange necke gybet ſtrangle y• ſhal neuer haue mercy thadmyral ballant ſuppoſed haue knowen hym ſayd theef proued whan ſayd thus went ſatte wyth came thyerey duc ardayne dyſſymyled chyere countenaunce manere whan thadmyral ſawe regarde ſo hydous moche abaſſhed ſuppoſed ben deuyl thyerry ſayd herkene admyral reteyne wel wordes charles noble emperour redoubted commaundeth thou ſende hym relyques thou bareſt awaye fro rome alſo ſende vnto hym hys baron whyche thou haſt thy power ellys thou ſure ſhal charles noble hardy curtoys good lyf thou ſure yf preſent wyth hys excerſyte moche ſone ſhold gyue buffet vpon thy vyſage ſyde ſetteth nomore thā olde hoūde dede roten apple incontynent tho ballant
