necke ſtrangle vylaynſly gybet yet nyght ¶vaſſal ſayd admyrall thou haſt ſayd grete folye mahommet god lyke wyſe ſhal doo thou haſt ſayd thy ſelf goo thou ſytte thy felawes ¶thenne hym came good ogyer danoys tofore hym ſayd admyral spaygne vnderſtonde charles mooſt noble humayn creature mooſt ryche wythoute comparyſon demaundeth rendre yelde hym relyques whyche thou haſt borne awaye ellys ſhal dyſmembre doo deye ſhamefully thadmyral beyng al wroth made hym ſytte wyth hym rolland courageous came tofore ballant thadmyral wythoute doyng hym ony reuerence ſayd hym thou ſaraſyn vnhappy curſed take hede wordes charles noble kyng emperour redoubted ſendeth thou byleue god iheſu cryſt maker al world gloryous vyrgyn marie moder baptyſed thynke rendre relyques whiche thou occupyeſt atteyneſt ayenſt hys wylle alſo ſee hys baron rendred delyuerd hole good poynte yf thou otherwyſe haue ſayd charles valyaunte ſhal make hanged theef thadmyral ſayd hym thou haſt rebuked blamed proudly ſwere mahoun god termagaunte ſhal ete tyl thou hanged ſtrangled thenne rolland anſwerd trouthe ſaraſyn yf thou abyde houre thou ſholdeſt faſte ouer longe thou ſhalt ſo doubte valure olde dede hounde drowned ¶guy bourgoyn came hym tofore ballant thadmyral ſayd hym thys manere charles commoundeth thou make hym ob • yſſaunce thou reſtore relyques hys baron thenne ſhalte thou wyſe man yf thou wylt byleue wyl wel counceyl byleue god iheſu cryſte whyche almyghty wych • ute ende wythoute begynnynge yf thou byleueſt counceyl thou mayſt grace thou ſhalt take thy robe thy hoſen thy ſhoon thy body goo thy 〈◊〉 bere thy body ſadel hors reſte tyl thou come byfore face charles humbly preſente thy ſelf hym crye mercy god thy maker almyghty thyn errours oultrages crye hym mercy honour god almyghty yf thou doo thou haue ſayd ſhal make hanged brente drowned ſhameflluy dye ¶the admyrall termyned araged tofore ſent anone brullant de mommyere sortybrant conymbres hys counceyl demaunded theyr aduys counceyl vpon theſe thynges aforeſayd anone tybrant ſayd hym syr admyral counceylle anone dyſmembred ſlayn ye may goo ryde ſtrengthe oueral come mormyonde charles penſyf yf ye may take hym ye ſhal put hym deth ¶after ye ſhal deſcende fraunce doo crowned kyng mahoun ſayd ballant ye haue wel ſayd doon deuyſe goo pryſon brynge wyth theyr felowes enterpryſe thus haue ſayd thadmyral entencyon make frenſſhe men aforeſayd tofore deuyſed ¶how moyen florypes al frenſſhe men ſaued lodged gydre relyques ſhewed thynges capitulo ix floripes curtoys ſhe wel ſecretly herde al debate foreſayd ſhe came hyr chambre ſalewed hir fader demaunded hym theſe knyghtes ſette parte thadmyral anſuerd doughter borne fraūce whyche haue ſayd wordes grete importaunce ful reproches haue blamed offended gretely telle ſay coū ceyl gyue ye ought ioyth doughter ſayd ſhal ſay fader ye wythoute longe taryeng ſmyte theyr heedes haue wel deſerued ſmyte theyr hondes brenne fyre without cyte doughter ſayd admyral ye haue ryght wel ſayd ryght ſoo ſhal doon goo ye pryſon brynge good fader anſuerd doughter tyme dyne yf ye wyl begynne iuſtyce ye may ete tyl mydday paſſed doughter ſought none thyng occaſyon fayr wordes accordyng wylle hyr fader thadmyral brynge al frenſſhe men gyder wyth pryſonners ¶and ſayd hyr fader gyue theſe frenſſhe men ſhal make theym wel kepte dyner ye ſhall iuſtyce wyth laſſe tedyacyon thenne people ſhal aſſembled ¶to whyche admyral conſented contente thyt hys doughter ſhold haue kepyng alwaye ſortybrāt knewe mutabylyte wommen thynconſtaunce ſayd ballant syr admyral noo thynge couenable vpon thys fayte ye ought truſte woman cauſe theyr mutabylyte ye haue oft berd ſay enſaumples alſo ye knowe trouthe many haue ben deceyued wymmen moche angry euyl content floripes wordes sortybrant ſayd horſon traytour deſloyal pariured yf thought ſhold torne ouermoche blame ſhold gyue ſuche buffet thy vyſage blode ſhold auale doun habundauntly theſe wordes thadmyral euyl contente thys debate therupon ſhe took frenſſhe men ladde 〈◊〉 hyr chambre wythoute ony lenger taryeng goyng waye syr naymes due ſayd god heuen kyng eternal glorye euer ſawe fayrer lady hys lyf moche wel ſhold inſpyred grace god ſhal haue hyr hys courage loue rolland euyl contente ſayd naymes hondred thouſand deuyls hath maad ſpeke loue tyme ſpeke ſuche thynge due naymes ſayd thus syr rolland dyſpleſe one amerous douȝter ſayd aſſembled plede one ageynſt alſo ſone wythin chambre doughter made ſhette faſte yatrs anone rolland mette wyth olyuer enterbraced eche kyſſed wyth franke tender herte wepyng moch tenderly alle ſemblably rolland ſayd ala olyuer faythful felowe ſythe laſt ſawe ryght wel anſwerd olyuer eche demaunded theyr feates contreyes theyr lordes tydynges ye may thynke gladde eche al togyder good poynte moyen florypes fayr lady whyche dyd grete ſocours cryſtendom whan hyr hyr wyſedom dyſcreſcyon captayne cryſten fayth moche toucheth excerſyte bataylle deſtroye myſcreauntes paynyms ben founded alle togyder ſurete whyche fyrſt comen hondes theyr enemyes mortall ¶but grete ſcyence eſchewe wylle woman whan effecte ſhe putteth hyr entente thynge hert dyrectly draweth taketh regarde ende entente onely ſhe may achyeue hyr enterpryſe determynacyon florypes retched noo thynge ſhe myȝt haue tydynges certeyn guy bour goyne whome ſhe gyuen hyr hert contente cryſtened loue hym thys fayr florypes whan ſhe ſawe theſe baron gydre ſhe ſayd lordes wyl ye alle one • coorde promyſe fayth loyalte ye ſhal ayde helpe ſhal demaunde toward ye ſhal truly bere endeuoyre ryght gladly anſuerd due naymes alſo ye ſhal aſſure v ſhal ſurete withoute ony doubte ony man lyuyng ſhe contente contente promyſed fydelyte whan doon doughter came duc naymes knowe demaunded hym hys name duc ſayd hyr madame called naymes bauyere man counceyllour charles emperour redoubted ala ſayd douȝter kyng ſory ſhe came rychard demaunded hym named anſuerd hyr dame rychard normandye doughter ſayd hym mahomet curſe thou putteſt deth tyme corſuble myn vncle loue theſe thou ſhalt daunger florypes came rolland prayed wold telle hys name named rolland ſayd ſone duc myllon neuewe charles ſone hys ſyſter anone doughter cryed hym mercy kneled doun hys foot rolland toke hyr ſwetely vp ¶after doughter ſayd ye knowe ye haue promyſed ſhal ſay myn entencyon trouthe loue knyght fraunce • boue al world whyche named guye bourgoyne wold gladly haue tydynges rolland ſayd ſwere hede ſyght bytwene tweyne ſpace foure foot meſure seynours ſayd ſhe praye may knowe hym gyuen hym alle playſyr rolland anſuerd ſayd ſyr guy bourgoyne come ye hyther thys mayde receyue hyr ioyouſly guy bourgoyn anſuerd god forbede euer ſhold take wyf yf ſhe gyuen charles themperour ¶whan florypes vnderſtode hym anone ſhe chaū ged colour ſware mahōmet hyr god yf gaynſayed ſhe ſhold make alle hanged necke gybette rolland enhorted guye ſhold hyr wylle vpon aduaunced hym hath graunted thenne florypes ſayd ſone god cryſtyante preyſed honoured haue tofore myn eyen mooſt gretteſt playſyr euer myn hert deſyred loue ſhal byleue iheſu cryſt ſhal baptyſed ſhe approched hym treate lytel deſyre hir hert ſhe durſt kyſſe hym mouthe hys chekes chynne cauſe ſhe paynym thenne florypes ioyouſly grete loue came vnto cheſte opened tofore baron ſpredde fayr cloth ſylke ſhe dyſcloſed ſhe wed relyques whyche haue ſpoken tofore emonge whome gloryous crowne wyth iheſu cryſte crowned tyme hys paſſyon holy naylles whyche perced hys holy handes foot ſayd rolland loo treſour ye haue ſo moche deſyred whan frenſſhe men ſawe thus tofore relyques ioye alle wepte moche tenderly one wente kyſſed knelyng moche humbly layed cheſte ben tofore ¶how lucafer neuewe admyral vyolently entred chambre ſlayn duc naymes blowyng cool capitulo x ballāt thadmyral beyng moche wroth ſyttynge table paynym fyers proude ſpecyal frende thadmyral named lucafer bandas ſayd thadmyral affectuouſly ¶syr admyral trouthe haue herde ſay fyerabras ſone ryght dere brother taken vaynquyſſhed whiche beſte knyght euer lyue thadmyral ſaid hym fayth ſhal hyde fro frenſſhe man hath conquerd hym whome maboun confounde brullant mommyere made grete deffence kyng sulye • ſoo wel brought v fyue gloutons fraunce knyghtes charles whyche ben pryſon ſythe ryght haue ſeuen whiche ben comen meſſagers fro ſayd charles haue vytupered blamed v gretelye reprochyng lawe deſpyſyng goddes florypes doughter hath conduyted pryſon ſyr ſayd lucafer ye grete folye wymmen al day lytel thynge ben chaunged torned fro theyr thouȝt neuertheles ſurete yf playſe comaundement ſhal goo ſhal knowe condycion goo forth ſaid thadmyral ye ſay ryght wel make doughter retorne wyth herupon lucafer moche proude replenyſſhed grete fyerſnes cam chambre douȝter frenſſhe men wythoute demaundyng opene dore lyfte vp ryght fote ſmote ſo ſtrongely wyth hys foot barres locke flewe vnto grounde whan florypes ſawe ſhe al abaſſhed anone ſayd rolland syr noble knyght ryght euyl contente vyolēce thus done ſhold huſband ageyn wylle requyre moche ye wyl playſyr ye wyl auenge thys dyſhonour complayne wythoute makyng ouermoche cuyl ſemblaunte whome rolland anſwerd doubte ye thyng madame departe hen ſhal knowe hath euyll doon promyſe bought neuer locke ſo dere ne pry ſhal brekyng herof hereupon lucafer entred chambre helde frenſſhe men al armed wythout ony doubte came fyrſt duc naymes whych dyſcouerd bare hede wythoute delyberacyon took hym berde drewe hym hym ſo boyſtouſly almooſt ouerthrowen hym ſayd hym whens art thou veyl lard hyde fro duke naymes anſuerd paynym bauyere contree ſpecyal counceyllour charlemayne al theſe baron ben al erles grete lordes ben comen ſhewe ballāt admyral meſſage fro ſayd charles redoubted emperour cauſe haue ſpoken hys entencion hath made v pryſonners neuertheles take hande berde ye haue holde longe ynough ye ſure ſay al thynke ¶the paynym anſuerd contente thy folye pardonned demaunde thy loyalte maner folke fraunce enterpryſe playes vſe whan royame trouthe ſayd duc whan kyng hath dyned wyl may goo playe hym lyſte somme ryde oute horſback ſomme goo feldes ſynge make good chere table cheſſe playſaunte game morne euery man gooth gladly hereth maſſe houre whan ſayd wel charytable gyue almeſſe y• poure peple largely cuſtomably alſo whan goo bataylle fyers hardy lyghtly vaynquyſſhed suche peple contreye cryſtente lucafer began lawhe ſayd god mahoun vylayne olde dotard thou arte thou ſpekeſt folyſſhly thynge ſo feat ne frenſſhe men valure yf blowe grete cole trouth ſaid duc herde neuer therof paynym anſuerd ſhal teche manere approched duc nyghe grete fyre goyng rolland made ſygne duc ſhold bere hym wel anone lucafer toke gretteſt bronde fyre blewe ſo ſharply fyre flewe alle aboute habundantly ſaid duc naymes muſt alſo blowe duc took bronde knewe wel manere paynym wold hurt hym approched hym blewe bronde ſo puyſſauntly fyl al flame came vyſage paynym ſuche wyſe br •• te al hys berde whan paynym ſawe almooſt wytte angre duc naymes wyth ſmote hym wyth brōde necke brake bone ſo raught hym wyth ſo grete myght eyen flewe oute hys •• ed grounde ſayd hym fals creature thou arte whome byſeche god confoūde thou wendeſt haue made muſe thy folyes 〈◊〉 wyth ſorowe rolland ſaid hym fayth ſyr duc 〈◊〉 wel playe blowe atre cole bleſſyd arme gaf ſtroke ¶lordes ſayd duc naymes yf haue maad hym vnderſtonde hys folye ye ought blame ye haue ſoon truffed wyth florypes curtoys came ner vnto duc naymes ſayd certes ſyr ye worthy honoured ſee wel lucafer hath charge playe wyth cole eaſe ſee wel remeueth wote neuer ſhal haue grete deſyre eſpouſe force wold haue fader gyuen hym neuer wold haue ſuffred father haue myn hede ſmyton ſuffred vylaynous deth ¶how counceyl floripes frenſſhe men dyſlodged thadmyral fro paleys wyth grete bataylle enchauntement gyrdle taken awaye fro douȝter ca xi florypes wyſe conſyderacyon lucafer whyche dede wel byloued wyth thadmyral ſayd frenſſhe men lordes knowe ye trouthe fader loueth thys man ony man lyuyng abydeth hym come dyner wyl eaſe tyl ſhal retorned yf aduenture knowe doon ye ſhal encombred aſſaylled al golde world ſhal redeme ye ſhal dede wherfore coūceyl ye doo arme put poynte take lyȝtly helmes ſheldes people armed moche redoubted vnarmed therfore wyl ye cloſed ne ſhette herin whan ye come paleys thadmyral see ye bere behaue ſoo ye mayſters lordes place thenne ſhal ye wel lodged whan doughter thus ſayd ryght wel contente preſtly armed gyrde ſwerdes aboute two two yſſued oute chambre goon corageouſly lyon boyſtouſly wulues hungry ſuche wyſe wold abyde onght ſore doubte haue grete fere went oute tyme ſonne wente vnder bytwene nyght day formeſt waye rolland folowed hym ryȝt fyerſly fyght roulland cryed hys felowes eche man ſhold hys parte ſlee al paynyms ſaraſyns fonde paleys whyche faylled roulland ſmote corſuble mortally olyuer put deth kynge coldroe ther one alle bare wel ſoupper whyche wel appoynted anone torned vp ſo doun caſte grounde cuppes golde ſyluer ſlewe ſowned place saraſyns goon therthe ſlayn dyſmembred lepe wyndowes whyche founden dede hewen ſholdres legges ſmyton thadmyral araged put hym ſelf flyght oute wyndowe lepe doun depe dyche rolland went whyche hym gretely hert ſuppoſed haue ſmyten hym atteyned marble ſtone wyndowe ſuche wyſe ſwerde entred foot depe brother ſayd olyuer admyral eſcaped fro certeyn anſuerd rolland therof euyl contente neuertheles dyd ſo grete portement bare ſo wel lordes mayſters chyef toure caſtel palays ſhetted faſt yates alle ſure wythoute daunger sauf myght haue noo mete paſſed lytel whyle admyral dyches al affrayed yf ſomme haue drawen hym oute neuer departed began crye men ſhold come hym drawe hym oute brullant mommyere ſor tybrāt conymbres drewe hym ſayd sortybrant syr admyral byleue another tyme alwaye attetayl olde dogge kepe thadmyrall anſwerd praye ſcorne nomore ſhal wel aduenge two monethes paſſed doo ſowne aſſaulte taſſaylle toure sortybrant ſayd reſon wylle doon nyȝt ouer nyghe myn aduys better abyde tyl morowe thenne excerſyte ſhal aſſembled werke ſurely thadmyral contente ſayd grete dyſplayſaūce ha fayr lucafer neuer ſhal ſee haue loſte 〈◊〉 ioye ye frenſſhe men accurſed ye ye haue taken hym awaye fro mahoun god whome haue gyuen lyf morne ſhal ſyege layed tofore toure ſhal neuer departe none euyl wether ſhal come thynge may tyl toure taken walles layed erthe ſhal make frenſſhe men drawen taylles horſes ſhal make florypes putayn brente fyre openly wel ſure ſhal yelde vytaylled ſcar • foure dayes parte knowe wel may haue ſocours mā ſomeuer holde ſtronge brydge mantryble may haue noo ſocours yf come ouer brydge parte charles ſhal haue noo tydynges baron ne ſhal knowe whether dede lyue lyberte ſubiectyon vpen concluded went lodgys tyl morne morne erly thadmyral ſen • e al hys ſubgettes concluded laye ſyege ſware holde ſeuen yere longe yf wylle thenne came ſo many paynyms contreye aboute theyr lodgyſes helde foure myle ſpace ye may thynke daunger frenſſhe men whyche twelue perſones onely none conduyte ne comforte wythin aſſyeged grete peryll famyne neuertheles alwaye ſaraſyns dyd gretely theyr deuoyr entre yet coude thyng gryeue thadmyral called one marpyn moche fals theef emonge alle humayn creature ſayd hym marpyn berde bere chynne yf thou mayſt ſoo moche ſtele awaye gyrdle florypes bereth ſhal rewarde gyue largely golde ſyluer thou ſhalt grete frende yf may haue ſure frenſſhemen ſhal ſone dede hungre thenne may nomore greue ¶that gyrdle ſuche vertu longe ſhold haue du red wythin toure wythin ſhold ne • er haue famyned syr ſayd theef abyde tyl nyght ſwere morne ſonne aryſe ſhal ſhewe gyrdle ſhal delyuer herupon whan nyght entred ſecretlye dyches whyche ful water paſſed ouer whan fote toure moche ſubtylly engynes mounted vp wyndowes entred toure took candel cam chambre florypes fonde faſte ſhette fals dyabolyke wor • e opened whan wythin ſawe al y• barōs faſt ſlepe made ſo enchauntements thynge myght awake thenne came florypes ſerched ſo pryuely took gyrdle gyrde hym ſelf wyth al thys behelde doughter al naked whiche moche fayre enclyned anone haue defouled hyr began take hyr aboute necke whyche ſodeynly awoke began crye moche ſtrongely called hyr maydens baron wherfore maydens came anone alabaſſhed aferde whan ſaw marpyn theef blacke moore mooſt hardyeſt began flee non guye bourgoyn herde boy florypes came hyr wyth hys naked ſwerde honde eſcryed hyr ſhe ſhold aferde ony thynge came ſo wel poynte yf come theef defowled florypes ſone theef herde hym ſprange oute bedde wyth grete haſte guye bourgoyne recountred hym gaf hym ſo grete ſtroke clefte hym myddel cutte two gyrdel candel quenched baron came whan ſawe werke theef dede threwe body ſee wyth gyrdle whan knowen ſtolen gyrdle loſte wyth hym ſee moche ſorowe loſſe ſoo noble iewel florypes wepte ryght ſore ſayeng loſſe gyrdle may neuer reconuerd neuertheles baron wyth fayre wordes comforted hyr ſuche manere alle contente ¶how baron aſſyeged toure wyth florypes hyr maydens ſuffred grete hungre goddes confounded capitulo xij whan day comen thadmyral ſawe marpyn thenchauntour retorne moche abaſſhed demaunded brullant sortybrant hys lordes counceyl ſhold doo conſydered marpyn retorned sortybrant ſayd syr admyral knowe ye certayn theef deed ſythe retorned comen counceyl ye doo ſoune trompettes taſſemble ſubgettes taſſaylle toure confounde cryſten men wyth ſlynges engynes doo caſte ſtones dartes enuenymed bleſſyd god frenſſhe men doubted thynge contynued ſyege whyle brede wyn began faylle baron maydens ſuche wyſe noo thynge ete thenne ſorowe maydens whyche ſo fayre ful compaſſyon ouer grete al deſolate emonge noble florypes moche dyſplay ſaunte neceſſyte frenſſhe men hyr ſelf hyr damoyſelles often tymes ſhe ſwowned fyl grounde dede guy bourgoyne hyr ſpouſe ſhold took hyr vp moche ſwetely recomforted hyr hys power ſayd hys felawes brethern lordes ye ſee neceſſyte ſuffre thre dayes paſſed ſyth ony brede yet greueth theſe damoyſelles ſelf ſay trouthe may lenger ēdure yf otherwyſe ye ſure leuer put body auenture hurt wounded mortally ſhold abyde wythin encloſed wyth thys melancolye wherfor ſay late v goo oute gete ſomme vytaylle better v deye wyth honour lyue ſhame al frenſſh men thoppynyon guy vpon florypes ſayd lordes wote wel god lytel power whan gyueth none ayde ne comforte ſay wel yf ye adoured goddes pourueyed mete drynke tofore ſhe fynyſſhed hyr wordes roulland anſuerd ſayd madame praye ye ſhewe v goddes ye ſpeke yf haue power ye ſay may gyue v mete drynke ſoo moche puyſſaunce fraunco come hyther ſocoure v ſhal al byleue wythout varyeng mayde ſayd anone ye ſhal ſee incontynent ſhe taken kayes ſhe ladde baron vnder erthe ſhewed goddes ſaraſyns whiche place moche noble precyous ryche grete mageſte appolyn mahoun termagaunt god margot iupyn many whyche alle maſſy fyn golde arabye enorned wyth many iewellys odoraunt bame encence many treſours aſſembled guy bourgoyne ſayd whan ſawe ſoo grete treſour lord god wold haue wende thys place ſo grete rycheſſe aſſembled wold god rychard normandye aupyn hys cyte roan ſhold wel accomplyſſhe wyth chyrche holy trynyte kyng charles thother goddes ſhold repayre ageyn y• chyrche rome whyche deſtroyed remenaunte ſhold make men ryche ſette good poynte florypes anſuerd ſayd syr guye ye ſpeke vylaynſly ayenſt goddes crye mercy adoure thende enclyne doo comforte guy ſayd vnto hyr praye madame ſee theyr eyen al ſlepe ye ſhal ſee may ne ſee therwyth ſmote iupyn ogyer danoys ſmote margot flewe 〈◊〉 anone alle broken wherfore roulland ſayd doughter trouthe madame ſee ye haue goddes worth fallen therthe ſee one remeue ne make ſemblaūte releue hym fro thēne forthon florypes al theyr goddes deſpyte byleued iheſu cryſte ſayeng thus ſee ſyr roulland ye ſay veray trouthe yf euer byleue wyl body come euyl ende good herte requyre god borne vyrgyn whome ye haue enformed ſende ſocours fraunce fynde maner gete vytalle ſatyſfye hungre ¶how peres fraunce went toure dyd grete bataylle recouerd twenty ſommyers charged vytaylle capitulo xiij whan florypes ſayd ſhe fyl doun erch ſwoune ſorowe anguyſſhe wherfor guy bourgoyn wept moche ſoroufully loue hyr hreupon olyuer courageous came tofore ſayd lordes aſſure god ſuffred deth creature humayn leuer body quartred ſmyton pyece • ſhold ſuffre pryſon ſhold fyght quyckely wyth paynyms ſemblably ſayd rolland wherfore wythout delyberacion ſette theyr ſheldes good poynte mounted horſluck aualed brydge wyth ſtedfaſt courage made redy whan alle afore toure marble rolland ſayd syr naymes ye ſyr ogyer • houeth one yon abyde kepe place retornyng may entre ſurely ¶the duke naymes coude take noo pacyence ſwerd thus syr roulland thynke ſo vnhappy perſone ne lygnage euer ſhold reproched euer ſhold portyer wyl doo ſo noo wyſe though olde yet torne myn hors harde ſynewes aud haue myn herte wel aſſured wyl hardy ynough ſmyte vpon myn enemyes whā tyme ſhal reqnyre ne doubte ye thynge therof rolland anſuerd ſyr ye ſay wel ye ſhal come wyth v thyerry geffroy one two ſhal abyde playſyr abyde encloſed neuertheles requeſt rolland thyerry abode geffroy whyche ſhetted yates ſurely baron wythoute whyche eche ſhelde tofore hym ſwerde hys hande wente muſtryng tofore caſtel thadmyral lokyng wyndowe knewe frenſſhe men wherfor haſtely ſente brullant ſortybrant come hym wyth whome ſayd baron ſubgettes frenſſhe men ben comen aud ſemeth wyl fyght yf al ſlayn ſhal euyl contente wherfore ſowne horne taſſemble people ye • ary ouer longe aſſone ſo doon grete multytude ſaraſyns aſſembled came aſſaylled frenſſhe men rolland helde durandal hys honde felowes came vpon maſtyn ſaraſyns ſuche furour lytel whyle moo hondred ſlayn vnhappy came ſocoure ſaraſyns thenne came claryon whyche neuewe admyral xv thouſand fyghtyng men know ye certayn tyme ſpayn noo ſaraſyn doubted whan baron ſawe hym come rolland eſcryed gherard ogyer guy noble knyghtes thonour god eche ſo deuoyr thys tyme wyth vyctorye may obtayne vytaylle maydens toure ſayd rolland ſmote hors wyth hys ſpores wyth durandal ſmote fyers paynym named rampyn ſoo myghtely cla • te hede body ſtroke wherof yt preſent abaſſhed thenne ſaraſyns doubted ſo ſtrongly rolland man durſt put hym ſelf tofore hym yf thought deye gherard mondydyer ſayd brethern lordes wyl haue playſyr honoured ty • e ſhewe hym often one vnhappy man halyaunt mā daūger wherfor word al theſe baron moche feruēt thā thende euery man ſhewed hym ſelf ſuche ouȝt y• batayll fynyſſhed day god wold baron fonde tour aforeſayd grete auenture ſawe paſſe caſtel xx ſommyers laden wyth vytayl ſay brede wyn venyſon vytaylles ynow paynym conduyted margote vnto ſaraſyns incontynēt ledars ſaraſyns theyr vytayl ſlayn anone baron due naymes wyllyam ſcot conduyted ledde forth rolland came auoyded place ſuch wyſe dryuen tour thyng doon without daunger grete payne ¶how guy bourgoyn taken ſaraſyns beten vylaynouſly demaunded thadmyral complayntes florypes made hym mater capitulo xiiij haue ſayd tofore baron fraunce thus wente theyr repayre ladde ſommyers afore ſayd came ſo grete habundaunce men armes partye kyng claryon merueylle thenne harde ſtronge recountre ſo moche due baſyn ſlayn aulbery hys ſone whan ſawe fader deye incontynēt fyl vpon hym ſlayn abode yet thys mooſt harm noble guy bourgoyn menaced kyng claryon auaūced hym ſmyte hym came hym ſo euyl paſſe hys hors ſlayn vnder hym paynyms ſodeynly enuyronned moo thā hondred knyghtes ſaraſyns whyche took hym took hys helme fro hys hede boūde hys eyen ſo ſaw nothyng ledde hym forth hys handes boūden behynde hym • backe whan guy ſawe hym thus deteyned began crye wyth hye voys ¶o ieſus veray god whych haſt made formed whyther goo euyl fortuned iheſus comforte noble charlemayn ryght noble emperour myn vncle thou ſhalt neuer ſee kyng claryon ſayd hym fayr frende thynge ſhal auayle thy cryeng ne thy brayeng ſhal delyuer al lyuyng admyral ſpayn thys day morne thou ſhalt hanged ye may wel thynke peres fraunce hys felowes euyl contente whan ſawe erle guye ſoo pryſonner ¶neuertheles dyd grete feates armes conſtrayned ētre tour aſſone deſcended yates barred eueryche went dyner thēne floripes cam anon rolland ſaid hym ſyr rolland requyre ye ſay ſyr guye bourgoyne huſbond become wote wel whan ye departed hen went wyth emonge thother ye ought brynge hym geyn ſhal neuer ioyous hert tyl knowe rolland anſuerd ha florypes curtoys lady hym truſt ye certes ye haue loſt hym ye ſhal neuer ſee hym paynyms haue ledde hym maulgre v knowe wyl wyth hym florypes heeryng theſe wordes ſorowe anguyſſhe fyl erth alle ſwoune iiij tymes dede rolland whych wepte hyr oft releued hyr whan ſhe ryſen ſhe began crye hye voys baron fraunce god maad heuen erthe yf haue gny bourgoyn whome ought maryed ſhal yelde thys toure nexte day paſſed holy vyrgyn marye ſhold eſpouſed hym loue hym baptyſed cryſten ala loues haue ſone faylled ſorowe hath made wel forgete hungre haue theſe iij dayes ala vnhappy rolland myght ſee melancolye thys florypes promyſed hyr make hyr glad wythin ij dayes thēne atte fertheſt ſhe ſhold ſee ſyr guye hyr playſyr ſhe ſhold thyng doubte therof knowe ye ſurely ſayd rolland leuer quarterd ſhold come ageyn ſhal rendred deth ſhal ſore auenged madame ye knowe wel ſorow wepyng may brynge hym ageyn ye wote wel thre dayes paſſed ſyth ete haue purchaced vytayl v theſe damoyſelles whome ye ſee pyte late v take pacyence lytel quantyte contente entretiene lyf ye ouȝt knowe myght recouure ſommyers vytaylle cauſe trouble guy bourgoyne whyche deteyned pryſoner rolland ſaid thys baron daruoyſelles thanked god al fedde ſuffyſauntlye prayſyng lawdyng god deuoutelye late v ſpeke lytel guye bourgoyn whiche ledde tofore admyral moche troubled dyſcolourd chaūged vyſage ſayd guye cauſe eten thre dayes tofore yt daūger felte hym handes enemyes tofore admyral al deſpoyled armes thēne appyered body wel membred ballant demaunded name barō anſuerd admyral fere ſay trouthe called guy bourgoyn ſubgette crowne fraunce coſyn germayn rolland valyaunt man ought wel doubted ballāt anſuerd knowe wel ynough vij monethes goon douȝter hath grete loue dyſpleſeth gretely know wel ſhe loueth thā ony man lyuyng loue haue loſt many men grete facion put tour chyef ſtrengthe al contreye yf al yolden ageyn ſhortly y• ſhalt quarterd ſhort tyme dyſmēbred ouer demaūde yt thou ſay trouthe ben encloſed tour haue ben aſſaylled ſo daungerouſly guy anſuerd gladly ſhal ſay thou wel ſure rolland valyaunte olyuer felowe ryght courageous thyerry duc ardayne rychard normandye gherard mundydyer naymes dne bauyere baſyn genewey ye haue ſlayn grace god helpe charles deth ſhal dere ſolde thadmyral ryȝt euyl contente menace guye wherfore moche fyers ſaraſyn took hys fyſte ſmote guye vyſage ſuche wyſe blood yſſued oute hys noſe mouth habūdantly wyth ſtroke guy ſette fyre angre furour lefte forthwith quartred holden toke ſame ſaraſyn heyre wyth one hys handes wyth hande • e ſmote hym vpon grete bone yt necke behynde ſtrake wythoute moeuyng hande foot fyl doun deed grounde tofore admyral ¶ballant ſoo euyl contente wyth broke al enraged deth paynym myſpryſyng guy doon hys preſence tofore eyen cryed loude voys ſhold takē aſſone ſayd worde ſaraſyns wulues enraged whyche wyth theyr foot handes al bete hym ſuche wyſe knewe ſlayne hym yf admyra • commaunded theym ſhold put deth ſuche manere • paynyms purpoſed haue hanged guye bourgoyne ſeeyng cryſten men whyche ſocoured hym myȝtely capitulo xv guye bourgoyn wel bounden ſtraytly thadmyral ſente come hym brullant mommyere sortybrant conymbres many coū ceyl ſayd frendes praye ye gyue counceyl ought wyth thys pryſonner whyche dothe ſo grete reproche deſpyſyng ye ſee knowe syr ſayd sortybrant ſhal gyue good connceyl yf ye wyl byleue ye ſhal doo reyſe vp galowe tree nyghe dyches toure whych pryſonners fraunce morne ye ſhal hange pryſoner ſee ye haue ſecrete place nyghe vnto yt ſaid galowes thouſād turkes wel armed good poynte ſure freyſſhe men ſo hardy oute meſure whan ſhal ſee felowe hanged ſhal come oute ſocoure hym peple ſhal hydde buſſhement ſhal come take thenne ſhal ye haue al ſurely wyth playſyr counceyl approued thadmyral good therwyth wel content wherfore wythoute takyng ony delyberacy galowes made afore ſayd ryght nyghe place lytel wode lete put therin ſecretly xx fyghtyng men comanded gouerned kyng claryon capytayns thadmyral made guy bourgoyne ledde xxx ſaraſyns vnto galowes whyche ceſſed bete ſmyte hym grete ſtaues whyche greued hym ſore bonde payne goo deye euyl deth meryte thy paſſyon take ſoule thy kepyng body taketh hys ende lyke haue nede thy helpe beſeche requyre counceyll comforte ¶o noble baron fraunco ye ſhal neuer ſee yf ye ſuffre hanged ſhal grete ſhame roulland fayr coſyn remembre ellys ſhal ye neuer ſee lyue thus ſayeng pyetous wordes rolland wyndowe behelde ouer lytel rocke ſawe galowes reyſed wherfore came hys felawes ſayd meruaylle moche thys meneth haue ſeen galowes ſette vpon dyches wote neuer purpoos doon whan ſeen duc naymes ſayd oute faute made hange guye bourgoyne forthwith ſaw hym comyng al deſpoyled ledde toward galowes knewe wel yf ſocoured reſcued ſhold hanged put deth • whan fayr florypes herde thē plede ſhe came wete whan ſhe ſawe galowes reyſed guy hir loue comyng huſbond ſo ſhamefully ledde ye may thynke eſtate ſhe reduced began crye noble knyghtes ſhal ye ſuffre guy bourgoyn felawe hanged tofore eyen truſte ye none yf deye ſame god fourmed ſhal lepe wyndowe ſhal deye deſperacyen ſhe came rolland kneled doun hyr knee kyſſed hys foot humbly ſayeng syr rolland thonour god requyre may playſe take payne reſcowe ſocoure loue guye ellys boſte woman thynke arme ſhal goo make redy horſes tyme ouer ſhort ſo playſyr god ye ſhal tyme thenne rolland felowes armed moche haſtely gyrde theyr ſwerdes ſheldes wente oute toure hors backe ſprange oute rode ony ferther rolland ſayd lordes thys houre lyeth deth lyf ſuche wyſe yf haue good conduyte loyal ſhal neuer retorne ne ben x paynēs ben innumerable grete force thonour god praye alwaye holde v togyder eche take hede moche may yf deuyded ſhal ſone taken hanged parte yf one v falle grounde preſtly reyſed leue hym lyf ne deth none faylle ſhal ſhal brynge gyder thayde god ſwere lyf long may holde durandal may kepe lyf body ye ſhal haue good deffendour waraunt lykewyſe ſayd al florypes anſwerd lordes ye may tarpe ouer longe ſhe went hyr chambre opened coffre whiche crowne iheſu cryſte moche reuerently kyſſed ſette theyr heedes wherfor good courage yſſued noo thynge dredyng puyſſaunce paynyms florypes hyr damoyſellys lyft vp brydge ſhette faſt toure ¶the noble peres fraunce fayr good ordenaunce wente toward galowes alonge medowes thynk ye haue begonne ſuche thynge werof ye ſhal repente thys hu •• made ſo impetuouſly mooſt hardy xxx helde guye began flee ſo haſtely pourſyewed xx ſlayn vpon wode camen makyng grete bruyt al afore came cornyfer meruayllous paynym vpon morel grete facyon began crye haye frenſſhe men dyſmeſured come ye ſocoure hym iuged thadmyral hanged ye haue enterpryſed grete folye al ye ſhal hanged wyth hym whan rolland herde paynym ſo ſay moche angry helde durandal hys hande came ageynſt hym wulf enraged neuertheles paynym ſmote ſhelde daungerouſly recouerd atteyned ſmote paynym ſo puyſſantly clefte hys heed doun body dede rolland came rennyng vnto galowes vnblynfelde vnbonde ſyr guye bourgoyne bad hym holde hym hym tyl armed roulland ſlayn another paynym guye beyng thaſſuraunce thother peres fraūce armed hym incontynent tharmes paynym helpe hys felowes mounted vpon paynyms hors thys doon wythoute grete payne meruayllous deffence made anone al ſaraſyns wode came vpon baron fraunce dyd grete inconuenyents neuertheles thayde god baron ſo good gouernement ſo entyer courage ſo meruayllous deffence puyſſaunce tyme put ſoo many ſaraſyns deth place al encombred al empeſſhed goo emonge whome guye bourgoyne dyd meruaylles armed conſeruacyon hys felowes dyd gretely hys deuoyr ſayd ſaraſyns ye traytres maſtyns ſhal ſhewe thys iourneye eſcaped fro handes thus fyghtyng made ſaraſyns withdrawe grete bowe draught thus fyghtyng ſyde moo thā ten thouſand ſaraſyns redy empeſſhe paſſage myȝt wythdrawe wherfore rolland holdyng durandal hys honde ſeeyng called al hys felowes ſayd lordes noo tyme wythdrawe v neceſſyte muſt auaunce v owne conſeruacyon yf may gete brydge doubte thyng thenne may wel ſaue v roulland sayd guye bourgoyne ye knowe wel toure haue noo thynge ete yf wythin ſhold lyue yet leuer haue body daungerouſly wounded fyghtyng vpon ſaraſyns deye hungre wythin wythoute daunger yf wylle god thys day ſhold deye al hys playſyr ſhal take worth good trewe knyghtes god baron hys oppynyon goon forth grete purpoos bere valyauntly •• beyng thys purpoos bere valyauntly ſayd florypes wyndowe toure ſawe guye bourgoyne hyr loue wherof ſhe moche ioyous cryed hym wyth hyr voys hit wold pleſe hym come hyr ſayeng yf ſhe ſyued proweſſe baron hyr fader thadmyral ſhold one hys daunger wherfor ogyer danoys ſayd lord haue ye herde nobly ſhe ſpeketh wel worthy doo hyr knowe ye ſhal capitulo xvj whan florypes curtoys beyng wyth hyr damoyſelles toure ſawe baron fraunce aſſured tofore caſtel ſhe cryed hem hyely ye lordes praye remembre gete ſomme vytaylles ye come entre herein came ayenſt baron holdyng hys honde dart ſtele fyrſt encountred rolland hytte hym ſhelde ſuche wyſe ſtooke al aſtonyed came ſoo paſſe touched hys fleſſhe ne hurte rolland came vpon paynym gaf hym good theſe tydynges enſure ſoule ſure paſſe thys daūger though ſtrengeſt caſtel fraūce bleſſyd richard god hath borne hym nobly ſemblably ſayd al felawes richard rode thus thadmyral made man come hym named orages made hym take dromedary haſtely comanded hym bere letter galafre kept ſtronge brydge mātryble charge rēne faſte dromydary may bere tomantryble ſay galafre wherfore ſuffred meſſagers charles come ouer brydge whyche haue doon v ſo moche greuaunce ennoyaunce thou wel telle hym ſwere mahon god dyd grete folye ſythe parte meſſager frenſſhe men goeth thyder yf recoūte meſſage charles myght happen ſhold put ſubgectyon therfore ſay galafre kepe ſoo wel brydge noo perſone paſſe ſay hym ouer yf otherwyſe ſhal put oute hys eyen make hym deye ſhamefully syr admyral ſayd orages meſſager ſhal commaundemente aſſure ſhal ryde moche waye one day ſhal foure dayes ryde hondred leghes contynuelly ſhal neuer wery thus departed admyral vpon dromydary taryed tyl came mantryble ſpake galafre moyen whyt hert cam tofore hym iiij rychard neomandye meſſager frenſſhe birons priſoners rode grete doubte ye may wel thynke ymagyne onely hym ſelf myght paſſe ſtronge daungerous brydge rydyng behelde behynde hym ſawe al contree couerd wyth men armes thus byholdyng theym ſore troubled hys mynde began crye iheſus kyng glorye thys tyme thou kepar body conſeruatour ſoule ſee wel declyne lyf yf put ſelf fyght ſhal haue hede ſmyton yf entre hydous ryuer ſhal conne paſſe ouer thus thys tyme muſte nedes deye yf force retorned felawes ſhold make grete defaulte therle rolland haue pormyſed faythfully doo deouoyr doo meſſage wherfore god maker wote ſay thy wylle fulfylled doon thou knoweſt myn entencion ſame gouerne beyng nyghe ryuer ſaraſyns maden grete bruyt comyng hym emonge neuewe admyral fyl doun therthe al deed took hys hors brydle whyche ryche golde went ryuage water helde rāne lyke quarel croſbowe rored lyke thundre ſuche wyſe galeye ne engyne myght goo ſurely vpon hyt ¶thenne grete contrycion hert recommaunded hym ſelf lord ſhold preſerue hym deth tyl ſayd hys meſſage emperour charles thenne god heuen neuer leueth hys ſeruauntes nede ſhewed vnto hym grete token loue charles rychard normandye beyng thys medytacyon thought paſſe ouer god ſente whyte herte paſſed tofore rychard comyng ye ought ryuage water moche hye ye hye man bynethe myght caſte vp ſtone wyth hys ſygne croſſe vpon body hauyng hys hert holy name iheſus myȝt perſeuere fro drede ſuche wyſe myght paſſe ouer ryuere ſoo toke water folowed hert paynyms ſeyng al abuſſhed troubled one durſt folowe hym fro incontynent water aualed retorned hys former eſtate beyng thenne paynyms made grete duel ſorowe cauſe myȝt haue meſſager ¶galafre whyche mooſt wroth werſt contente cam bridge aualed chaynes commanded paynyms vpon payne deth ſhold ceſſe tyl rychard taken ellys ſhold indygnacyon thad myral daunger loſte rychard normandye came ouer good poynte deuoutelye thanked god grace ſente hym ſomeuer ſemblaūt made ſayd ſyr emperour yf ye byleue ſhal gyue good counceyl ¶anone comaunde lodgys habytacyons take vp euery man truſſe hys gheer vpon ſommyers thynke retorne yf ye goo ony ferther ye ſhal neuer redorne contree aygremore moche ſtronge ſythe ballant admyral grete fyerſnes wyth hath alle paynyms ſaraſyus capytayns hys ayde cauſe fyerabras hys ſone deteyned maad cryſten ſo moche affectyoned ayenſt parte baron lyue enſure retorne fraunce haue lefte many chyldren parent ſhal wexe grete twenty yere ſhal bere armes thenne v ſhal come ſpayne conqueſte londes ſeygnouryes haue ganellon ſmyton wyth ſoo grete ſorowe fyl donn ſwoune ſpake ſpace grete houre wepyng bytterly ſayd hym ſelf ¶o poure caytyf vnhappy ſhalt thou yf thou retorne yu ſhalt dyſhonoured yet better loſe lyf thā thus ſhamed comen hym ſelf ſayd hys baron loo ye ſee counceyl ganellon gyueth whych wyſe may playſe yf retorne wythout takyng vengeaunce noble baron ben thus deteyned ſhal neuer man ſette ſhal ſhamed wyth good ryght machayre aulbery geffroy moo hondred whyche al parent traytres wyth ganellon mooſt parte alſo moche myghty gydre ſayd alle wyth one conſente syr emperour purpoſe ye otherwyſe ganellon hath ſayd hath ſpoken wyſely therfor conclude ye retorne fraunce wythout gooyng ony ferther ben xx thouſand haue made oth gyder ony thynge ye ſay ſhal goo noo ferther ſythe roulland dede haue loſte theyr comforte hym chyef conſeruacyon perſones charles al heuy anſwerd god heuen determyned yf retorne wythoute auenge baron ſhal doo pourely fythe haue ſuſteyned borne vp crowne imperyal wylle retorne wythoute auenge gaf ſuche counceyll loueth lytel ſee wel reyner gene fader olyuer aroos vp ſayd ¶o emperour yf thou byleue theſe wordes haue ben ſaid thy gouernaunce ſhal ſo euyl al fraunce ſhal waſted brought nought ſomeuer haue damage retche paſſe ouer lyghtly thenne partye traytres cam forth ſayd reyner gene ye haue lyed whiche ye haue ſayd yf bycauſe kyng preſent ye ſhold loſe hede ſhold ſmyton knowe wel ye fader garyn neuer pour man lowe condycyon alle lygnage ne ben people nought ¶the duc reyner myght ſuffre thys iniurye came hym ſmote hym wyth hys fyſt ſuche wyſe ouerthrewe grounde made many reproches ylle talent ſo moche yf kyng preſent made pee tranquylyte ſlayn eche anone moo thouſand lygnage ganellon fyerabras preſent blamed ſtrongely ſyde kyng ſware hys crowne yf ony perſone began bataylle fyght ſhold hym hanged theef attaynt ſomeuer eſtate thys aferde offende nomore ſpoken withſtandyng counceyl taken emonge ſhold put reyner deth ſone ſhold fraunce charles ſent come hym ſaid ye haue done grete ſhame yf amended fore ſhal opene iuſtyce alwaye nedes muſt kynge obeyed ſuche wyſe • ory hys knee cryed duc reyner mercy wold neuer haue doon yf appeaſe furour kyng charles thus maad pee themperour ſayd oppynyon yf torned backe ſhold hym grete dyſhonour therfor cam geffroy daulteuylle fader ganellon whyche ſayd syr emperour olde haue ſeen moche thynge wherfore ſemeth ye ought byleue wel ony perſone companye ye knowe wel ganellon ſone haue alwaye loued counceylleth retorne hath good ryght haue body alle bruſed beryng armes ye ſure tofore twenty yere paſſed chyldren fraunce ſhal grete myghty bere armes ſhal ſo grete companye lyȝte ye ſhal mowe conquere ſpayn auenge deth rolland hys felowes whan charles vnderſtode theſe wordes wepte bytterly ſaw force muſt ayenſt hys wylle retorne fraunce leue hys enemyes wherfore ſowne trompettes cryed retraytte anone artylleryes aſſembled harnoys truſſed wherof companye traytres ioyous many euyl contente thaffayres peres fraunce capitulo vj whan charles moū ted horſback waye retorne took remors rolland olyuer lefte oute otherwyſe deuoyr taryed ſayeng vnhappy may wel ſorowe whan leue men loue beſt world retorne fro whan ought good ryght auenge ſhal reputed fool ſore blamed rolland haue loued may euer vnclle ſo longe lyue moy ſee deth auenged god deffende euer bere crowne hede ſeen pouerte fayte thys ſayeng almooſt fyl ſwoune erthe dyſplayſaunce moche heuynes tyme ala ſayd charles rolland moche euyl auyſed whan conſented thou ſholdeſt goo thadmyral wel cauſe al perdycyon makyng thys heuynes hooſt made ſoo grete bruyt retourne meruaylle thus began ryde forth emperour loked toward eeſt ferre ſawe rychard come rydyng vpon hors ſore rennyng helde hande ſwerde al naked wherfor emperour ſente come hym mooſt gretteſt lordes hys companye made thooſt tarye goo ferther forth ſee ſayd yonder • myng man horſback maketh grete haſte ledeth hys ryght ſyde fayr courſer thynketh ſemeth hys rydyng rychard normandye praye god almyghty thys day ſende tydynges rolland baron alyue thenne hooſt taryed anone came richard whyche maad hys hors lepe moche gentylly tofore kyng whome ſalewed moche humbly thenne charles ſayd rychard normandye sone noble baron hyt wyth bycomen neuewe rolland myn baron ye come allone alyue dede telle praye rychard anſuerd syr emperour rolland whan departed fro al hole good poynt aygremore ſtronge toure byſyeged ballant admyral ſpayne fader fyerabras aboute hondred thouſad ſaraſyns knowe ye certayn thadmyral man moche fyers terryble whyche hath ſworn god mahoun termagaunt ſhal neuer departe fro then ſhal hāged necke ſyde baron haue wyth floripes curtoys doughter thadmyral fayreſt euer ſeen whyche hath hyr kepyng relyques ye ſoo moche deſyre haue ſende worde ye ſhold come ayde ſaue theyr lyues yf pleaſe remembre ye ſhal mowe conquere contreye ſpayne goodes ynough grete conſolacyon kyng charles thenne conceyued wel ganellon traytre ful wyckedneſſe neuer hys counceyll ne ſayeng ſhold herde ne alowed hys courte ſawe wel hym abode rolland hys felowes ſhold haue dyed gentyl rychard ſayd kyng toure whyche byſyeged ſtronge wel garnyſſhed vytayl defende ony whyle yf may holde vj dayes ſhal make thadmyral dye al hys complyces syr anſwerd rychard ſhal ſay trouthe haue noo vytayl grete ſwerde thadmyral meruayllouſly fyers ful cruelte hath people multytude innumerable whyche holde ſpace two myle town ſtronge habyteth alſo thys ſyde toun brydge mantryble paſſage moche daū gerous walles cyte ben made marble cymented fortefyed toures renneth ryuer ryȝt hydous whyche named flagot depthe ij ſperes lengthe renneth ſo faſt brayeth noo bote ne ſhyppe may paſſe theron brydge half myle longe myddes tonre marble ſo ſtronge may beten doon yate garnyſſhed kepte wyth barryers yron faſt locked ¶the portyer kepeth thys plaſe paynym hydous grete maſſyf ſtronge felonnous whyche better reſembleth deuyl ony man perſone blacke pytche boylled hath x thouſand knyghtes companye wher fore wote wel force may paſſe ony aſſaulte may doon doubte yf paſſe engyne ſubtylte may goo ouer brydge force may noo thng byhoueth v paſſe guyſe marchaunts ſomme v ſhal wel armed vnder clothes aboue ſhal man tel cloth theyr ſwerdes vnder ſhal come v grete • ommyers charged marchaundyſes ye wyth al chyualrye ſhal tarye lytel wode euery man grete poynte whan haue goten fyrſt gate ſhal ſoune blowe myn horne wyth motye ye ſhal come thus ſhal haue paſſage playſyr god ſhal come entencyon thys counceyl wel approuued kyng charles whyche ofte bleſſyd rychard cauſe ſo wel ſayd thenne reſembled al peple ſtandardes reyſed loryflam dyſcouerd rychard took hys hors gaf duc reyner wente bonde heye graſſe gydre made truſſes vpon many ſommyers guyſe marchauntes euery man wel armed vnder hys cloke ſwerde gyrde ſo take theyr horſes thende ſhold eſpyed nombre v hondred knyghtes alle man grete facyon dryue tofore ſommyers good enterpryſe rychard went tofore chyef enterprenour due howel nountes folowed guye de hallee ryoll du mauns duc reyner fader olyuer whyche rode forth wythout taryeng charles wyth alle hys barōnye abode wode tofore haue maad mencyon ¶how moyen counceyl rychard normandye wyth iij baron ſtrong brydge mātryble wōne wythoute grete payne maner man galafre capitulo vij themperour charles hondred thouſād men abode wode tofore ſayd rychard normandye hoel naūtes ryoll reyner peple whyche valyaunte theyr perſone waye goo toward mantryble ladde wyth aquantyte ſommyers charged whan felowes rychard ſawe ryuer flagot ſo roryng thentree cyte mā tryble ſo ſtronge brydge ſoo daungerous paſſe yates barred enchayned ſo wyth yron moche abaſſhed come thyder aſſaulte alle puyſſaunce cryſtendom myght entre place aualed brydge chaynes yron ryol demaunded rychard may place anſuerd knowe ye thys ſtrongeſt cyte bytwene thys acre ſame cyte 〈◊〉 thouſand men armes hoel nauntes alle afrayed commaunded hym ſelf god prayeng hym kepe theyr perſones rychard ſayd lordes wyl goo byfore ſhal ſpeke fyrſt whan haue paſſed fyrſt yate ſee ye take clokes ſmyte vpon paynyms ony thynge happeth ſee one faylle ryol anſuerd doubte ye whan emonge ſaraſyns ſhal doo deuoyr ſhal appyere yf doo ſay wyl ye reclame recreaunte repute rebouted theſe wordes haſted theyr ſommyers toward brydge galafre ſawe fro ferre ſtode reſtyng hym nygh fyrſt gate helde honde grete axe fyn ſtele bended affyled noo ſyde cutted thys paynym grete fonrmed ſo hydouſly ſuche repreſentacyon ſemed better deuyl reſonable perſone eyen al enflammed lyke fyre blacke boy led pytche hys necke large grete noſe half fote longe cere ſo grete myȝt conteyne wel half buſſhel whete hys armes longe croked foot ſtode ouerthwart remenaunte hys body lothely ynough ballāt thadmyral loued hym moche neuewe grete confydence hym gaf hym kepyng brydge mantryble cauſe mooſt ſtrengeſt paſſage al march contreye ſayd paynym coneſtable al londes thadmyral wherfore neceſſarye none frenſſhe men ſhold haue knowen hym yf ony knowen ſhold neuer none haue eſcaped ſhold haue ben dede thus thenne whan mantryble rychard paſſed afore whan entre gate galafre came hym ſayd baſſal ye wherfore come ye hyther ¶rychard whyche wyſe chaunged langage began aragon ſayd syr marchaunte whyche cometh fro taraſton wyth theſe marchauntes brynge grete quantyte draperye wyl goo fayres helpe mahon whome goo preſent marchaundyſes yf aygremore ſhold ſoiourne gyue thadmyral ſomme precyous yeftes brynge theſe marchauntes ben wyth ben al eſclaues knowe langage wherfor fayre ſyr praye aduyſe v may beſt waye ought goo galafre anſuerd knowe ye kepar brydge paſſages fyfty myle aboute longe ſythen paſſed hereby xii glotons fraunce whiche meſſagers emperour charles yet owe theyr trybute theyr paſſage neuertheles lord thadmeral kepeth pryſon one day eſcaped preuyly away theef whiche rode vpon hors beſt euer ſawe paſſed ouer thys rennyng water whyche alſo ſlewe coſyn kyng claryon whome grete melancolye wold god mahon vpon thys brydge ſhold cleue hym vnto myddle bely wythout haue ony mercy pyte hym syth tyme thadmyral doubteth treaſon ſone fyerabras whyche hath renyed mahon paynym lawe become cryſten commaunded thre tymes ſhold ſuffre ony perſone lord knyght ne ſeruytour paſſe ſhold ſerche wel al knowe condycyon theym come thys waye therfore wyl knowe ye rychard heryng bowed hede ryol du maūs hoel nauntes reyner gene goon forth ouer brydge whan galafre ſaw began doubte ſayd ſhold nomoo entre auaunced hym drewe vp brydge nomoo wythin foure whyche dred ſayd grete fyerſte ye ouer bolde hardy entre herein wythout commaundemente therfor ye four ſhal ſette pryſon come alſo morn ſhal ſende pryſoners lord thadmyrall doo playſyr take mantellys clokes wyl ſee ye haue vnder ye ſeme people euyl thus ſayeng toke hoel cloke drewe hym therby foure tymes aboute god ſayd ryol may longer tarye ſee hym thys iniurye coſyn yf ſuffer lenger confounded therwyth threwe cloke ſmote vpon paynym ſo ſtrongely armed myght hym harme ſauf ſmote lytel hys ere rychard reyner ſemblably caſte theyr clokes eche ſwerde theyr hondes ſmote gydre vpon galafre gof hym many ſtookes heed ne body myght hurte armed hyde olde serpente harde maylled ¶thys paynym angry ſuppoſed haue ſmyton ryol enhaunced hys axe grete heuy alſo ſharpe ryol ſawe ſtroke come habylle lepte ſyde ſtroke ſmote vpon grounde ſuche wyſe hyt claffe marble ſtone whyche ſtroke lyghted ha god heuen ſayd reyner ſmyteth oultrageouſly al abaſſed puyſſaunce thys deuyl may conquere ne gryeue thus ſayeng took grete braunche tree whyche longe ſtronge aduyſed marked paynym wel ſmote hym therwyth ſuche wyſe made hym ouerthrowe therthe whan ouerthrowen maad crye ſo hye hydous ryuer roches made grete bruyt wyth thys voys paynyms mantryble moeued aſſembled lytel whyle redy armed moo x thouſand thenne grete cōmocyon rychard normandye ranne yate brydge aualed doun drawe bridge thenne entred v hondred knyghtes whych foure baron brought wyth entre gate paynyms encountred grete medle recountre many mortal ſtrokes gyuen many ſlayne hurte rychard took hys horne ſowned hyely thre tymes charles themperour vnderſtood wel whyche wood aforeſayd al puyſſaunce euery man horſback moche redyly one ceſſed renne tyl came brydge ¶ganellon whyche traytour bare hym valyauntly fyrſt cam brydge wyth hys confanon reyſed loyalte trouthe hym ne hys kynneſmen endured longe laſte book ſhal playnly ſhewe playſyr god ¶now force ſtrengthe bataylle charles entred mantryble galafre ſlayn wythſtondyng alory traytre contrarye hym many mater capitulo viij thentre mantryble moche hurt people confounded wel frenſſh men ſaraſyns tyme themperour bare hym wel whome attayned wyth hys ſwerde named ioyouſe muſt nedes deye ſmote ſo rudely day alway hym ganellon whych dyd wel hys deuoyr dyches towne depe ful water wherin many drowned ¶thus charles paſſed tofore hys people ſawe galafre ye groūde dede ſemed better deuyl reſonable perſone helde alwaye hys axe hys honde wyth whyche ſlayn thyrty frenſſh men emperour ſeeyng harme doon frenſſhe men anone commaunded ſlee hym ſo moche ſmote hym wyth ax ſtones ſlewe hym bruyt noyſe ſoo grete fyue myle aboute anone knowen brydge mantryble taken conquerd wherfore came l thouſand ſaraſyns gyue ayde cytyzeyns mantryble deſtroye f • enſſh men walles towne marble ſoo ſtronge ſemed thyng impoſſyble conquere deſtroye ¶to thys medle came geaūt moche fyers named ampheon wyf named amyotte ſhe departed fro hyr geſyne ſhe borne two ſones whyche iiij monethes olde two foot brode breſte ten foot longe thyſtorye ſayth thys geaunt opened gate helde honde club yron grete maſſyf whan paſſed yate wyth hys voys tenebrouſe dyabolyke cryed charles kyng fraūce wyl bere wyth hym relyques ſaynt denys mahon whyche comforte ſelf better hym olde dotard parys late hym knowe certaynly yf thadmyral may haue hym ſhal neuer haue mercy hym ſhal hym flayn hanged alle quycke brenne hym fyre thus ſpoken ſmote doun many f •• nſſhe men wyth hys club 〈◊〉 ¶in thys recountre 〈◊〉 founded ſo grete multytude dede men lefted men paſſe charles whych ſawe facyon deſcended lyght hys hors alle wroth hys courage ſette hys 〈◊〉 tofore hym wyth hys ſwerde 〈◊〉 hys hande hys baron came hym ayenſt graunt 〈◊〉 kyng aſſembled charles wyth hys ſwerde ioyous ſmote hym ſee myghtely clefte hym two pyeces myghtely recouerd hys ſtroke maad hym falle erthe ſoo deed wherfore saraſyns moeued affrayed people enraged ſmote vpon frenſſhe men dartes plombetres engynes mortal ¶and thenne charles cryed ſocours aſſemble hys people wyth crye came hym rychard normandye reyner gene hoel nauntes syr ryol du 〈◊〉 whyche alle courage lyke vnto lyon theſe foure baron wyth charles made paynyms remeue reentre ageyn force towne man tryble anone turkes whyche moo x thouſand cam yate ſhette makyng grete defence bowes ſhotte beſyde came whyche kepte paſſages wel thyſtorye maketh mencyon fyue thouſand alle coude fynde maner lyfte vp brydge conſerned kept ayenſt ſaraſyns frenſſh men grete bruyt thys recountre though charles doubted noo meruayſſe knewe wel yf ſaraſyns lyfte vp brydge yate towne poſſyble hym haue paſſed ouer ſeyng reyſe vp toward yate grete barres yron ſuppoſed haue paſſed wyth moche wooful herte began wayle roulland neuewe hys felowes ſhold neuer haue ſeen ¶rychard normandye conſyderyng thys eſcryed ſayd syr emperour honour god maye thynke deſtroye ſmyte doun theſe turkes god ſhal ayde helpe v ye knowe wel none ſo franke ne valyaunte wyl acoward hym ſelf ought deſpyſed wyth good ryght ¶and praye god confounded ſuffreth hym ſelf taken lyue dye afterward leuer hewen pyeces retorne wythoute late v auaunce v nede eche man proue hys ſtrengthe valure hys perſone wyth theſe wordes grete courage entre towne charles reyner hoel ryol rychard theſe fyue onelye eche wyth ſwerde hys honde ye ought wete entred wythout grete ſlaughter turkes paynyms charles ſeyng come grete multytude ſaraſyns cryed larme ſocours moche hye furyouſly ganellon vnderſtood hym hym grete pyte wythſtondyng laſte founde hym good came geffroy eſcryed haateuyle fader hys kynneſmen whyche armed moche rychely nombre vij al came fote aſſayle yate turkes maad grete deffence wyth brondes barres yron mortal ſhotte many dede hurte people ſayd ganelon thenne alory traytre ſayd ganellon fayth ben grete foles late v thus deye ſuffre thys torment ſayd ganellon yet late v goo departe charles wythin wel empeſſhed god forbede euer departe thou mayſt wel ſee hym reyner wel auenged contradyctyons made v theyr ſubgettes alſo euyl deth mote deye foloweth ony ferther may wynne fraunce eaſe wylle holde wythout contradyctyon seen baron wyl v contrarye ganellon anſuerd god glorye forbede euer ſhold ſuche trayſon ryȝtful lord holde hym al londes ſeygnouryes ſhold holden ouer vntrewe man yf conſented hys deth haue none cauſe ought deuoyr hym whan alory vnderſtood hym enraged almooſt angre ſayd ganellon ye veray fool ye tarye whan ye may wel aduenge yf themperour charles ſlayn al baron ſhal haue theyr heedes ſmyton thus ſhal aduenged al enemyes therfore loue come ganellon anſuerd god forbede euer ſhold traytre lord ne leue hym vnholpen doo deuoyr ayde hym louer dyſmembred ſhamed blamed dede ¶of theſe wordes euyl contente alory alſo geffroy daulteuyle ſuche 〈◊〉 grete debate emonge vpon came fyerabras good araye grete poynte began crye charles ¶the traytre anſwerd syr ye ſhal neuer ſee hym wythin encloſed 〈◊〉 dede fyerabras anſwerd ye emonge doo 〈◊〉 ye ſocoure ye hym thys nede ye may reproched treſon wyth good ryght bygan crye ſocours ayde moche lowde hys voys frenſſ • men came wythoute ony taryeng belfroye fende fyerabras ganellon thenne lefte traytres entre brydge ¶and fyerabras thene wel ioyous whan ſawe brydge drawen thenne ganellon dyd gretely theyr deuoyr entre cyte whan wythin traytres ſawe toun wōne manere gretely theyr deuoyr entred foot ſmote doun wyth comunelye grete habundaūce blode runne thurgh towne oute dede bodyes eche man meruaylled ſawe paynyms cryed brayed wulues enfamyſſhed whan ſawe coude reſyſte ſente admyral ſhold ſocoure cryed mahon termagaunt wold come theyr ayde dyſcomforted ſorowfully put oute theyr habytacyons robbed pylled theyr rycheſſes goodes deſtroyed thus doyng meſſager departed ſecretely goo aygremore tacompte telle tydynges theyr deſtructyons ¶how amyotte geanteſſe wyth ſythe greued gretely cryſten men hyr two ſones baptyſed emperour charles capitulo ix whan mantryble taken many ſtrokes gyuen whan amyotte geanteſſe knewe herd crye cytezeyns whiche troubled blacke pytche boylled hyr eyen rede brennyng fyre ſhe grete vyſage croked hye lengthe ſpere gretely affrayed deth hyr huſbond alſo aferde hyr ij ſones whyche ſhe late delyuerd ſoo ſhe rage lepte hyr hous fonde ſythe trenchaūt meruayllouſly ſharpe cam vpon frenſſhe men ſo impetuouſly ſhe maad grete dyſcomfyte ſuche wyſe none durſt wel approche hyr kyng charles ſceyng thys euyl contente deth hys peple demaunded croſſe bowe whan lende ſhotte ſo ryght atteyned hyr bytwene browes ſo ſhe fyl doun deed erthe began caſt oute hyr throte flamme fyre moche hydous neuertheles ſhe ſmyton ſo wyth ſtones thynges ſhe neuer moeued wherfore yates towne deffences kepte ne defended charles dyd wylle alle ¶grete rycheſſe founde fayre towne ſubgettes emperour charles wel refreſſhed gold ſyluer whiche habounded thadmyral ballant cauſe place ſo ſtronge ſure layed grete treſours kyng ordeyned ſuche manere bothe grete ſmale wel contente wyth hym abode thre dayes dapartyng deſtrybutyng goodes degree qualytrees hys ſubgettes charles wente ſportyng ryuer flagot caue founden ij ſones yonge chyldren fornamed geaunteſſe amyotte whome wel ioyous baptyſed one named roulland olyuer dyd wel nouryſſhed wythin two monethes bothe founden dede theyr heddes wherfore themperour euyl contente neuertheles ſame tyme whyche moneth may ſtronge cyte mantryble taken put ſubgectyon charles made come hym rychard normandye reyner gene hoel nauntes ryol mauns took counceyl ſhold kepe brydge paſſage man tryble tyl deſtroyed ballant admyral delyuerd oute pryſon peres fraunſe rychard anſwerd ſyr emperour ſemeth ſhold good hoel ſyr ryol ſhold abyde kepe yt brydge toun wyth fyue thouſand men lyke rychard ſayd ſo doon ij abode hurt men heled theyr leyzer ſowne trompettes hooſt emperour began departe toward aygremore ſo moche peple ſo grete eſtate merueylle thus wel theyr waye emperour wente vpon lytel hylle byholde peple ſubgettes ſeeyng multytude lyfte vp hys eyen heuen ſayd lord god creatour whiche thy grace 〈◊〉 ſyr haſt made lord conduytour thys people wyth ryght good hert gyue thankynges lande thou haſt gyuen grete puyſſaū •• ſythe wylle commaundemente ſayd thus bleſſyd hym name iheſus took forth hys waye ſayd emperour hys companye hondred thouſand men wel fyghtyng admyral fyghtars thyrtene contreyes frenſſh men rode forth rychard normandye auaunte garde duke reyuer anone tydynges came thadmyral galafre ſlayn mantryble taken dyſcomfyted wherfore ſwowned ſorowe cryed haroo man fro hym ſelf ſayeng ha ha god mahon thy power nought curſyd god recreaunte thou art nothyng worth moche fool truſteth whan thou ſuffreſt men ſlayn haſt conſented dyſhonour wel ſee whych ouȝteſt wel haue doon contrary thys ſayeng admyral took clubbe two handes ranne mahon goddes ſmote mahon ſoo grete ſtroke vpon heed fyl doun al broken yf thadmyral paynyms wel abuſed myght knowe clerely theyr infydelyte fals creaunce inuoke ymages ſpeke ne gyue comfort haue conſolacion lytel vnderſtondyng lacke wytte alſo contrarye nature gyue fayth helpe thynge made hande man neuertheles sortybrant conymbres ſeeyng deſolacyon thadmyral counceylled hym moche myght chaſtyſe hym ſelf iniurye doon mahon thadmyral ſaid hym may enclyne hym obeyſſaunce seeyng charles hath wonne puyſſaunce cyte ſtronge tour mantryble laſte comforte kepe mooſt ſure sortybrant anſuerd syr admyral ſende forth eſpye wete yf hooſt charles cometh hyther ageynſt yf ſoo late v ryde ayenſt hym bataylle gyder yf ye may late hym taken hange hys people brenne without ony mercy pyte thenne ye may caſte tour theſe glotons kepe ſmyte heed fyerabras thy ſone aydeth whan admyral ballant herde sortybrant conſyderyng hys affectyon humbly retorned mahon purpoſyng ſad ¶how peres fraunce aſſaylled ſtrongely euer toure quaſi put therthe recomforted holy relyques adoured mater capitulo x sortybrant prayed ſoo moche thadmyral hym olde kyng coldroe tempeſted hym brullant de mommyere thyniurye doon mahon tofore al ſhold make amendes admyral beyng content affectyon ſware ſhold encreace mahon augment thouſand weyȝt cuſtome fyn gold precyoſytees anone dyd ſowne trompettes inſtrumentes ſowne whome aſſembled ſaraſyns inuumerable al armed admyral maad brynge hys engynes throwe grete ſtones tour brynge doun alſo deſtroye frenſſhe men hys doughter thus feruent euer ben cam taſſayle toure laye theyr engynes therto wyth whych paynyms made fyue grete hooles toure thurgh leſte myght paſſe carte caſe whan thys doon olyuer rolland wyth theyr ſheldes fore theyr ſwerdes theyr hondes ſtode wyndowes yet ſoo hardy emonge abuſſhed wythſtondyng good wylle defende alway hym myght attayne ſtones thynges ſoo hurte hym dyd nomore hurte ne damage doyng thadmyral cryed frendes ſubgettes doo deuoyr brynge erth thys partye praye god tyme yeue grace doo wel promyſe yf ye put oute thys aſſaulte ſhal ſhewe thyng wherof ye ſhal joyeful wyth tho thordes baron goo ſmyte hewe doun turkes ſo vygorouſly many dede hurt whych hole walle ſmote wyth ſtoones tour ſuche wyſe caſte dyches drowned anone goten thoo hole ſtopped faſte encloſed florypes axed fyrſt naymes duc vauyere thyerry duc ardayne ſayd lordes tyme ye promyſed ſware ye ſhold ony thyng ayenſt wylle wyl ſhewe crowne iheſus two nayles nayled croſſe whyche haue long kept baron heryng thys wepte ioye ſworen hyr ſhold thynge hyr al loyalte trouthe florypes wente thenne fette lytel coffre moche ryche fayre tofore ſhe opened aſſone relyques taken vnwounden ſeen grete clerenes meruayllous reſplendyſſhour thenne baron kneled doun erthe deuoutely ſmytyng ſelf breſtes contrycyon hert duc naymes bouyere fyrſt kyſſed wyth grete reuerence came wyndowes paynyms mounted hye aſſone ſawe tombled doun ye grounde dede al broken whan naymes ſawe ſayd lord god glorye whyche mayſt al thynge thanke gyue lawde prayſyng ſee wel knowe theſe ben reliques whome haue ofte ſpoken incontynent took hardynes courage ſayd hys felawes brethern recomforted ſo ſhal neuer fere ye doubte paynyms ne ſaraſyns florypes remyſed relyques coffret honeſtly thadmyral ſawe prynces wyndowes hys doughter wyth ful fals entencyon eſcryed hyr wyth hye voys cauſe wold vnderſtonden florypes fayr doughter ſee wel thou art grete fool thy fader whan truſted ful folyſſhe counceyl put thyn hande moyen thy lāgage fyrſt pryſoners haue herde ſay longe ſythe man truſteth woman thyng importaunce moche fool neuertheles thy puterye ſhal endure longe truſte ſwere ſhal departe loue thou haſt wyth glotons fraunce wythoute pyte ſhal doo brenne al florypes herde theſe wordes took baſton honde made ſygne though ſhe menaced hyr fader wherfore thadmyral ſeeyng began ſowne godre hys peple comaunded ſhote loſe inſtrumentes ayenſt toure ſuche wyſe anone grete partye walle ouerthrowen therthe thenne barōs doubted moche vpon walle rolland olyuer ogyer went chambre mahon appolyn termagaunte margotte goddes paynyms whyche moche ryche rolland took appolyn whyche heuy threwe vpon paynyms olyuer lyfte vp termagaunte ogyer margotte ſmote wyth ſaraſyns ſuche wyſe attayned dyd neuer hurte whan thadmyral ſawe thus goddes vytupered throwen took ſuche angre ſo grete yre hys courage ſorowe tombled doun dede man erthe sortybrant moche ſorowe took hym vp many wepte made grete deſolacyon ſorowe thadmyral ſayd lordes frendes ſhal euer frende ſpecyal byloued yt wyl aduenge ſhame theſe glotōs haue doon goddes sortybrāt dyd grete payne recomforte hym ſayeng ſhort tyme ſhold auenged al ſeen toure broken moo xv partyes hon ſayd admyral thou haſt wel forgoten mooſt nede thou faylleſt thou arte ſo olde thou doteſt haue ſeen day y• haddeſt grete puyſſaunce ¶sortybrant anſuerd syr ye haue euyl cuſtome whan ye ſpeke ſo euyl ayenſt mahon ye knowe wel neuer borne ne neuer ſhal ſo good god gyueth v pleute wyn goodes alſo ſhal doo v whan hath bythought hym yer euyl contente ſtroke ye ſmote hym noſe abyde lytel tyl better aduyſed frenſſhe men ſhal reſde vnto ſoo ye ſhal holde pleaſed vpon theſe wordes mahon broughte tofore hym deuyl entred hym whyche ſayd thys manere adoured hym admyrall ryche lord ne dyſcomfort ſowne trompettes horne aſſemble peple aſſaylle toure thys tyme ye ſhal take frenſſhe men wyth theſe wordes thadmyral al reioyced alle thengynes inſtrumentes dyd ſette ayenſt tour threwe ſtones maad grete ſhotte ageynſt toure whyche thenne al broken almooſt al ouerthrowen peres fraunce ſeyng thys grete doubte daunger wythout cauſe neuertheles ogyer danoys ſayd hys felawes loyal companyons replenyſſhed fydelyte ony payne doubte deth emonge v late none founde wyth ony treaſon ne ſuffre entre hym ony euyl thought infydelyte cowardyſe ye ſee yt tour gooth groūde almooſt theſe ſaraſyns medſed wyth v touchyng ſwere god maker tofore ſoule ſhal departe fro body yf haue puyſſaunce holde hande cortayn ſwerde ſhal make ſo grete dyſcomfyture theſe paynyms euery man ſhal meruaylle theſe wordes rolland byhelde durandal olyuer eueryche byhelde theyr ſwerdes alle renewed wyth ſtrengthe courage al wyth one wylle goon vpon ſaraſyns dyd ſuche dylygence allewaye lordes toure made ſaraſyns theyr enemyes goo abacke florypes conſyderyng theyr affayre ſorowful ſocours cam alſo remembryng menace hyr fader thadmyrall guye bourgoyn recomforted hyr alwaye ſuche wyſe al ſhe contente ¶how peres fraunce tydynges yf thooſt charles admyral alſo paſſyon ſuffred al humayn creature yelde baron whyche holdeth hys pryſon alſo reſyques longe tyme haue demaunded hym yf wyl ſhal leue hym hys contreye hys landes yf wyl doo otherwyſe ſhal make hym mortal warre ſhal take hym mercy ganellon contente goo thyder allone took ſette helme mounted vpon hors named gaſcon henge hys necke ſhelde wherein paynted lyon went vale ioſue haſtely anone taken turkes kept paſſage whan knewe meſſager ſpeke thadmyral troubled hym lete hym goo taryed tyl came tofore thaby tacyon thadmyral lente vpon ſpere knyghtly countenaūce moche reſembled baron grete valure ſay wel hys meſſage whan thadmyral knewe comyng came hym thenue ganellon ſpake hardyly hym manere saraſyn take hede vnderſtonde meſſager noble charles kyng fraunce ryght myghty emperour ſendeth worde thou renye forſake mahon thyn goddes dyabolyke byleue iheſu cryſt redemptour al worlde whyche took hym humanyte ſuffred deth cruel bytter tree ofithe croſſe redeme al world yf thou ſo thou art aſsured onely deye alſo leſe thy londe ne none thy good thou ſhalt alwaye byloued hym fyerabras thy ſone yf thou wylt accorde herto withſtande knowe certayn charles thou art deffyed al thy people yf thou wylt ſaue thy ſelf thynke flee wythdrawe fro thys contreye yf thou may taken holden thou ſhalt delyuerd daungerous deth alle thy ſubgettes ſhal dy ſmembred ſlayn ſhal gyue thy royame thy rycheſſes ſcruauntes therfore aduyſe wel whan thadmyral herd hym almooſt rage hys wordes deſtreſſe angre took ſtaffe ſmyte meſſager ſayd hym gloton payllard thou art dyſmeſured thy langage mahon whome yeuen thys tyme thou haſt ouer hardy lytel loued charles whan ſente thou ſhalt wel ſure thou ſhalt neuer recounte hym thy meſſage ganellon ſeyng wel ſure wyth took hys ſwerde whyche heuy ſharpe gaf wythal ſtroke buillant mōmyere breſte ouerthrewe fyl foot admyrall whyche ſeyng eſcryed moche ſtrongely tauenge hym thenne wyth thys voys aſſembled moo fyfty thouſand turkes take ganellon whyche wherof al baron al reioyced made good thyere whan ij hooſtes recountred al coutrey ſhone theyr armes ther ſo many haue ſayd tofore kyng charles made ten bataylles fyrſt ordeyned rychard normandye due reyner gene ſecond ganellon thyrd lory fourth geffroy fyfthe machayre vj hardre ſeuenth amangius viij sampſon ix tenthe conduytour charles kyng eche bataylle x thouſand men armes wel fyghtyng atte thys day ſhal ende thy lyf ſubgettes lyf wythoute faulte thou ſhalte yolden thadmyral alle thy centreye ſhal deſtroyed themperour herde wel theſe wordes wherfore alle furye lete renne hys hors came ageynſt paynym attayned hym ſuche wyſe hys harnoys brake drewe hys ſwerde neuer lefte hym tyl dede fro then ſpere came turke kynge pyetrelee ſmote hym breſte fyl deed erthe whan ſpere broken dyd grete loue hym hath gyuen beyng knowleche lyf wel requeſyte nedeful haue honour penerence hath made heuen erthe al therein enhabyteth wherfore good ryght ſuperyour abouen al grete abuſyon compryſed hym gyueth fayth hope whyche hath made wyth hys hondes mater dede inſenſyble hath neyther reſon ne ſoule thy goddes dyabolyke whyche may ne gyue conſolacyon theyr ſubgettes wherfore warne helthe thy ſoule preſeruyng thy body thy goodes thou take waye alle theſe iniquytees peruerſe affectyons byleue holy trynyte fader ſone holy ghooſt one onely god almyghty byleue ſone god repayre thoffence formeſt fader adam deſcended thys world took humanyte wombe bleſſyd vyrgyn marie whyche al pure wythoute ſpotte byleue artycles fayth obeye kepe hys comandementes hath gyuen v helth byleue taken iewes enuy hanged croſſe redeme v fro paynes helle byleue hys reſurrexyon aſcencyon hys body gloryfyed thynges holy bapteſme whyche hath eſtablyſſhed wyth ſacramentes yf thou wylt thus byleue thou ſhalt ſaued thou ſhalt neyther loſe body ne goodes thadmyral anſwerd wold thynge ſo ſware deth ne lyf wold leue mahon themperour holdyng naked ſwerd ſayd hym yf forſoke mahon ſhold put hym deth fyerabras ſeyng thys kneled doun therthe prayed hys fader emperour ſayd thadmyral fered deth ſayd contente fonte ſhold bleſſed charles glad dyd make redy fonte wyth fayr water fayr veſſel byſſhop wyth mynyſtres chyrche dyd halowe fonte made alle redy whan thadmyral vncladde byſſhop demaunded hym ſayeng syr ballant forſake ye mahon crye ye mercy god heuen treſpa •• byleue ye iheſu cryſt ſone vyrgyn marye whan thadmyral vnderſtode theſe wordes al hys body began tremble deſpyte iheſu • ſpytte fonte caught byſſhoop wold haue drowned hym fonte plonged hym therin ne ogyer haue whyche letted hym yet notwythſtondyng 〈◊〉 gaf grete ſtroke thadmyral blood came oute hys mouthe habondantly 〈◊〉 al abaſſhed preſent thenne kyng ſayd fyerabras ye ſpecy •• frende ye ſee fader wyl neuer cryſtened alſo oultrage hath doon fonte excuſed muſt dede dyſmembred ¶fyerabras requyred hym yet lytel pacyence yf wold amende hym thenne ſhold doo hys wylle ¶florypes doughter admyrall ſeeyng thys ſayd ¶o syr emperour wherfore delaye ye ſoo moche put thys deuyl deth retche though put deth ſo onely may haue guye bourgoyn myn huſbond haue ſo moche deſyred fyerabras anſwerd fayr ſuſter ye haue grete wronge enſure ſwere god whiche hath made wold loſt two membres condycyon good criſten man baptyſed byleued iheſu cryſt ye wote wel fader whiche hath engendred v ought honour hym loue hys helth ye wel obſtynat whan ye haue hym noo pyte wepyng ſayd fader mooſt dyer fader praye better aduyſed loue hym hath fourmed hys ymage whyche iheſus god ſouerayn lyke themperour hath ſayd leue mahon hath neither wytte ne reaſon ne noo thyng gold ſtones wherof compoſed yf ye thus ye ſhal v grete ioye enemyes ye ſhal make frendes ballant anſuerd fool glouton thou art ſpeke nomore therof thou art al oute reſō ſhal neuer byleue hym deyed v c yere goon acurſed putteth hys byleue aryſen fro deth lyf mahon god yf hors back taken ſhold angre charles fool whan fyerabras al vnderſtonden hym ſaid charles ſhold wyth hym hys playſyr good ryght ought deye anon themperour demanded wold ſlee ballāt vnmeſurable felon thenne ogier preſent hated hym hert forthwyth ſmote heed fyerabras pardōned hym gladly thenne florypes ſayd rolland ſhold accomplyſſhe promeſſes bytwene hyr guy bourgoyn rollād anſuerd ye ſay trouth ſayd guye ¶syr ye remembre wel wordes loue hath ben bytwene curtoys florypes kepe trouth promeſſe hyr guy anſuerd redy al themperour wold haue hym doo charles contente thenne anone afore theym alle ſhe deſpoyled vnclad hyr baptyſed beyng al naked ſhewed hyr beaute whyche ryght whyte wel formed ſo playſaunt amerouſe formoſyte hyr perſone euery man merueylled ¶for ſhe hyr eyen clere two ſterres fayre forhede large hyr noſe ryght wel ſtondyng myddes vyſage hyr chekes reed whyt medled hyr browes compaced lytel ſhadowe colour vyſage hyr heyr ſhynyng golde ſoo good ordre accumyled henge bynethe hyr knee hyr mouth wel compoſed attemperat roūdenes ſmal longe necke hyr ſholdres fayr thornes ionqnes ſee wyth grete deuocyon ſhewed adoured many wepte wayled deth lord iheſu cryſt grete deuocy contemplacyon byſſhop deuoute wyſe wold preue lyfte vpon hye ayer wythdrewe hys hond crowne abode ſelf ayer thenne byſſhop certefyed peyle preſent crowne iheſu cryſt hede tyme paſſyon thenne euery man honoured deuoutely ſoo grete odour eueryche meruaylled byſſhop took naylles whyche god hys haudes foot perced preued proued crowne tofore ſemblably abode ayer myraculouſly charles ſeyng al thanked humbly god ſayeng ¶o lord god eternal whyche haſt gyuen grace haue ſurmounted myn enemyes infydels haſt put ſette waye gyuen conduyte fynde relyques whyche haue ſo longe deſyred humbly rendre gyue thankes prayſynges contrey may wel ſay ſhal perpetuel honour hit poſſode haue thys precious cryſtendom ¶and thende thou ſholdeſt knowe place thou ſholdeſt goo thou haſt ſeen heuen ſterres dyuyne magnyfycence obteyne ioye gretter glorye heuen haultayn grete puyſſaunce thou ſhalt ſurmounte kyng charles knewe mandement gadred grete peple came onely wyth ijm knyghtes honour grete ſtrēgth whan foure myle nygh cyte aygolant al kynges tofore named left people ſecretly came vnto mountayne nygh cyte accompanyed wyth xl knyghtes onely fro thys place ſaw cyte cauſe wete yf multytude peple departed ſoo ſhold deceyued neuertheles vpon thys montayne lefte hys people ſecretly took hys clothes hath ſente v vnto leteth wete v comen lyke thou haſt comanded accompanyed wyth fourty knyghtes onely ought doo thenne come hym wyth xl knyghtes withoute moo yf thou wylt accomplyſſhe holde thou 〈◊〉 called carantha ſōme cryſten men planted theyr ſperes grounde eſpecially morn ſhold • ye obteyne crowne glorye marters god morne fonde ſperes al grene myraculouſly leued ful bowes wherof criſten men moche ioyous myracle raught deye ye cryſten fayth mayn tenyng name god cutte theyr ſperes wente bataylle put many ſaraſyns deth thende ſlayn martred cryſten men moo iiijm whyche ſaurd heuen tyme hors ayenſt criſten men wythoute makyng grete rebellyon ſaraſyns anone ſlayn put deth thenne kyng aygolant experyence fore made afermed fayth lawe cryſten peple better ſure certeyn lawe paynyms ſaraſyns thus enclyned cryſten fayth dyſpoſed hym receyue baptym moene without fayn tyſe vpon demanded tryews ſurete goo come charles graunted hym wyth good hert thus atte houre tyerce whan charles dyner aygolant entencyon ſee charles hys maner mete knowe hys aſtate yf vayllerous ſoo grete armes bataylles alſo came pryncypally baptyſed ſawe charles hys table grete magnyfycence behelde ordre hys peple ſawe ſomme habyte knyghtes grete prynces habyte channons monkes aſked ſo certefyed euery ordre canſe theyr eſtate ſawe parte y• halle ſyttyng groūde xiij poure perſones dyned ete dyd charles cuſtom wold take repaſte tyl xiij poure men worſhyp lord xij appoſtles toke hede theſe poure men ſatte grounde without wayl ryght poure habyte dyned al ſoroufully demaunded people charles anſuerd ſayd goddes peple meſſagers lord iheſu cryſt whome ſuſteyne thonour hym xii appoſtles hym gyue refectyon corporel aygolāt ſaid certeynlye ſerueth euyl hys lord y• receyueth meſſagers thys manere ſee wel ben aboute good poynt wel arayed wel ſerued mete drynke ſeruaūtes thy god lyue rourely euyl clothed ayenſt y• colde ben withrawen ferre fro thy dooth grete ſhame lord receyueth meſſagers manere ouer ſee wel lawe whyche thou haſt ſayd good holy thy werkes thou ſheweſt fals valewe herof aygolant moeued troubled entendement beyng put alle fro hys purpoſe toke leue kyng retourned hys peple renounced baptyſed ſente word charles begynne warre ageyn y• morne ſtronge euer doon tofore ¶of deth aygolant peple moche cryſten peple ſlayn concupyſcence ſyluer cryſten men founden dede myracle x whan charles ſawe aygolant come baptyſe hym moche ioyous whan retorned forſoke euyl contente took aduys vpon pour men whyche ſayd meſſagers god pouerte named fore holde ſo none honour theyr mayſter emperour remembred wel peple god ought receyued honeſtly honourably holden ſcrued wherfore poure men fonde thexcercyte dyd wel clothed honeſtly gaf mete largely took ſuche cuſtome hym ſelf faylled pour peple receyued honour companye vpon thys purpoſe day folowyng ſaraſyns put bataylle fyght ayenſt cryſten men grete fyerſte ſoo grete deſtructyon day ſaraſyns cryſten men empeſſhed lette blood ranne ſo habundantly rayned many dayes water blood wherfore aygolant ſeyng deſtractyon people doubted nothyng deye aduaunced ſo hym ſelf ſlayn put deth criſten men entred cyte pampylone put deth al ſaraſyns fonde therin thenne kyng cybylle kyng cordube ſaued ſelf wyth ſomme ſubgettes thys cryſten men ful couetyſe haue gold ſyluer ſaraſyns deed retorned whan wel charged laden wyth golde ſyluer hauoyr kyng cybylle kyng cordube took hede therof wyth al meyne came couuertly vpon cryſten men put deth moo thouſand ¶thus may knowen ardeur concupyſcence cauſe deth ſoule wythoute vyctorye god dyſplayſaunte ¶on morne tydynges came ſo many ſaraſyns ſlayn ſpecyally aygolāt vnto prynce nauarre named furre wherfore ſent charles haue batayll ordynayre charles ſo noble ſo puyſſaunt ſo truſtyng god whan faught cryſten fayth refuſed hym day bataylle whyche aſſygned bothe partyes charles put hym ſelf prayer prayed god deuoutely pleſed hym ſhewe cryſten men ſhold deye bataylle day folowyng whan euery man armed fyght wylle lord charles ſawe ſame day ſygne croſſe alle rede vpon ſholdres behynde vpon theyr harnoys whan charles ſawe thanked lord compaſſyon theyr deth cauſe valyaūce theyr perſones thenne ſent bare thenſigne made goo hys oratorye ſhette faſt therin ende ſhold take deth day thenne wyth al hooſt went ayenſt thooſt prynce furre longe furre hys people deſtroyed put deth whan doon emperour came hys oratorye vyctoryous vpon hys enemyes fonde al ſhette wythin dede expyred thenne knewe wel alle marked croſſe aſſygned day receyued heuen glorye crowne marterdom apperteyned charles prolonge theyr helthe wherfor wel ſymple wyl put hym payne eſchewe paſſage whyche mayſtre ¶of feragus merueyllous geaunt bare awaye wyth hym baron fraunce wythout daunger • olland faught wyth hym capitulo xj
