allone hym took hym wyth one hande put hym vnder hys arme wythoute doyng hym ony harme bare hym vnto hys lodgys dyd put hym pryſon made nomore doo bere hym dooth wulf bere lytel lambe heyght thys geaunt twelue cubytes face cubyte brode noſe palme longe armes theys foure cubytes long backe hand thre palmes longe ogyer borne thus awaye charles ſente raynold daultepyn whan feragus ſawe hym bare hym awaye lyghtly charles abaſſhed ſent tweyne wete conſtayn rome therle hoel geaūt took one wyth ryght honde lyft honde bare bothe tweyne pryſon hys lodgyng euery man myght ſee yet charles ſent tweyne ſemblably bothe borne awaye wythoute ony wythſtandyng contradyctyon whan charles ſaw foot man al abaſſhed durſt nomore ſende ony perſone man myght reſyſte hym roulland whyche prynce al thexcerſyte charles cuyl contente thys geaunt vyctoryous came charles preſented hym ſelf goo fyght wyth hym charles wold graunte hym laſt force conſtrayned gyue hym lycence roulland made hym redy cam tofore feragus anone taken reteyned hys ryght hande lyke geant layed hym tofore hym hys hors whan rolland ſawe taken borne awaye ſoo vylaynſly took gtete courage hym ſelf called name iheſus help hys ayde torned hym ayenſt feragus took hym chynne made ouerthrowe fro hys hors fyl grounde rolland alſo anone aroſe eueryche took hys owne hors roulland whyche moche habyle courageous drewe hys ſwerde durandal came ayenſt geaunt gaf ſoo grete ſtooke paynyms hors carf hym ſondre myddes paynym fyl erthe feragus beyng euyl contente hys hors dede took hys ſwerde ſmyte rolland ſlayne hym wyth ſtroke yf attayned hym aſſone lyfte vp hys arme haue ſmyten rolland • oulland auaunced hym ſelf ſmote geant vpon arme whiche helde hys ſwerde ſuche ſtroke hys ſwerde fyl grounde wherof feragus grete deſpyte ſuppoſed hanc ſmyten hym wyth hys fyſte attayned rollandes hors ſuche wyſe ſlewe hym thus bothe two fote whyche wythoute ſwerd begynnen fyght wyth theyr fyſtes wyth ſtones contynuelly tyl houre none wherfore bothe wery took tryews gyder one accorde vnto morne ſhold fyght wythout ſpere wythoute hors vpon eche went vnto hys lodgys ¶how morne rolland feragus foughten dyſputeden fayth moyen feragus ſlayn roulland capitulo xij ¶the next day folo wyng erly rolland feragus came felde bataylle geaunt brought hys ſwerde moche grete thynge worth rolland made prouyſyon grete ſtaffe clubbe ryȝt longe wyth whyche ſmote geaunt myght nowher hurte hym alſo ſmote hym grete ſtones rounde coude noo wyſe hurte ne entre hys fleſſhe maner •••• ceſſyd fyght tyl houre mydday geaunt wery demaunded iryews rolland ſlepe reſte hy lytel rolland dentente ſo noble ſo valyaunt whan geaunt layed went fet •• grete ſtone layed vnder hys heed ende myght better ſlepe reſte hys eaſe lytel ſlepte awaked ſatte vp noble rolland came ſat hym ſayd hym meruaylle moche thy feat thou art ſo ſtronge ſo terryble thou mayſt hurt ne woūded thy body ſwerd ne ſtaffe ne ſtones ne noo wyſe geaunt ſpake ſpaynyſſh ſayd hym world iuged erthe wythoute hauyng beatytude ne felycyte longe tyme ſone god ſecond perſone trynyte remembred hym valure ſoule whiche gyuen euery perſone deſcended fro heuen took humanyte ſuffred greuous paſſyon paynes beyng thys world hath gyuen enſeygnements ſtablyſſhed conſtry tucyons ſaue v pryncypally byleueth hym hys werkes parfyghtly baptyſed thys mortel lyf ſhal ſaued heuen thys fayth holde wyldeye feragus made hym many queſtyons fayth rolland anſuerd hym honourably euery poynte feragus ſaid manere thou art cryſten wylt mayntene fayth whyche thou haſt ſpoken paynym holde god mahoun v tweyne ſhal vayn quyſſhed ouercome late hys lawe holde nought noo valewe fayth hym vyctoryous late holden good trewe entyerly kepte obſerued valyaunt rolland contente ryght wel accepted hys langage thenne eche redy fyght anone rolland came hym feragus lyft vp hys arme ſmyte rolland moche malycyouſly ronlland ſawe ſtroke come vpon hym voyde lann •• hys ſtaffe ayenſt ſwerde wyth ſtroke ſtaffe cutte aſondre wythal geaunt ranne rolland hym doun vnder hym rolland conſyderyng myght flee ne eſcape called hys hert deuoutefy name iheſus yelded hym god vyrgyn marye anon repryſed ſuche ſtrengthe myȝt aroos lytel myghtyly repugned geaunte ſuche manere brought geaunte vnder hym thenne moche quyckly ſubtylly ſette hande hys ſwerde prycked hym nauyl therwyth anone aroos fledde al myȝt thooſt charles anone feragus felte hym ſelf hurt place cryed ſo hye lowde alle place aferd abuſſhed hys crye ſayd mahōmet god haue gyuen fayth come ſocour thou ſeeſt wel dye tary • noo lenger hydous voys ſaraſyns camen hym bare hym awaye theyr armes beſt wyſe coude vnto hys lodgys tyme rolland comen alle hool ſauf vnto charles forthwyth cryſten men went impetuouſly vpon saraſyns bare feragus entred cyte ſo moche dyd geaunt dede came pryſon valyauntly took oute ogyer reguault conſtantyn hoel pryſonners ¶how charles went cordube kyng ſame place kyng cybylle abode deſtructyon ca xiij thys aforeſayd kyng corbude kyng cybylle ſent charles ſhold come cordube fyght anone charles knewe came thyder wyth al hys puyſſaunte whan nygh taſſemble bataylle ſaraſyns maad moche ſubtyl wylde thyn • e tofore saraſyns horſback •••• ned men fote whyche •• ſieres counterfeyted black rede horned berded lyke deuylles deceyue cryſten men eueryche theſe 〈◊〉 men bare hys honde lytel belle thentre bataylle began ſowne make ſuche bauyt aſſone horſes cryſten men ſawe ſo countrefayred ſowne belly ſo im ••• uouſly began flee diſcenge aferde ſuche manner man myght holde theyr horſes force muſt flee wythdrawe charles deuyſed remedye morne blynfelde horſes couerd theyr eyen wyth clothes ſtopped theyr eres ende ſhold ſee ne ſaraſyns dyſguyſed countrefayted whan came bataylle manere ſpared ſlewe doun ryght put ſaraſyns deth tyl mydday yet al vaynquyſſhed carte myghty grete reſyte make grete empeſſhement theyr enemyes engyne drawen wyth viij ox warre thre vpon ſtode hye ſtandard theyr enſygne theyr cuſtome payne deth noo perſone ſhold retorne ne goo aback thyng long ſtandard ſtode vpryght hereof charles enformed wherfore moche puyſſauntly rode thurgh ſaraſyns tyl came ſtandard ioyouſe hys ſwerde holde hym none otherwyſe thenne charles ordeyned ſpayne certayn hys baron kepe ſuche wyſe none durſt aſſaylle ne make warre alwaye vyctoryous enemyes puyſſaunce ledde alſo dyſcreſcyon hys perſone put ſette good eſtate good warde ſpayne went ſaynt iames wyth fewe people whan ſuche criſten men fond rewarded dyd moche good punyſſhed ſuche apoſtates maner peple ſuche fonde vntryewe dyſobeyſaunte iohan theuangelyſt brother ſaynt iames ſone zebedee thus saynt iohan lodged ryght ſyde saynt iames hys brother lyft ſyde thenne accompliſſhed peticyon moder hyr two ſones gloryouſe frendes lord iheſu apparente theſe thre place ben honoured pryncypally cauſe ſynners may haue theyr recours tamende theyr lyues put awaye theyr ſynnes obteyne pardon forgyuenes fyrſt theſe iij appoſtles ſay saynt peter saynt iohan ſaynt iames haue preceded companye iheſu cryſte whan thys world haue ben called hys ſecretes haue mooſt contynued wyth hym thus good ryght place whyche haue conuerſed contynued theyr lyues holy lyf hys myracles hys marterdom hys ſepulture good ryght ought memorye thorugh vnyuerſal world ¶the ſecond parte thyrd book conteyneth x chapytres ſpeketh treaſon made ganellon deth pyeres fraunce ¶how treaſon compryſed ganellon deth cryſten men ganellon repreuyd thauctour capitulo primo tyme cezarye two kynges ſaraſyns moche myghty one named marfurrius bellegandus brother whyche ſente thadmyral babylonne ſpayne whyche vnder kynge charles made hym ſygne loue ſubgectyon went hys commaundement holyly vnder ſhadowe decepcyon themperour ſeyng cryſten gete ſeygnourye ouer ſente ganellon whome fyaunce ſhold doo baptyſe ellys ſhold ſende hym trybute ſygne fydelyte contre ganellon traytre went thyder dyd meſſage many deceyuable wordes ſente hym ageyn charles wyth xxx hors laden gold ſyluer wyth clothes ſylke rycheſſes iiij hondred hors laden ſwete wyn gyue men warre drynke alſo ſente aboue thys thouſand fayr wymmen ſaraſyns grete poynte yonge age al thys ſygne loue obeyſſaunce gaf ganellon xx hors charged wyth gold ſyluer ſylkes precyoſytes hys moyen ſhold brynge theyr hondes companye charles yf myght doo thenne ganellon ſurpryſed wyth thys fals auaryce whych conſumeth alle ſwetenes charyte perſones haue gold ſyluer rycheſſes made pacte couenaunte wyth ſaraſyns bytraye hys lord hys neyghbours cryſten brethern ſware wold faylle thenterpryſe merueylle moche ganellon made thys treaſon wythoute hane cauſe coloured ne iuſte ¶o wycked ganellon thou comen nobleſſe thou haſt doon werke vylaynnous thou ryche grete lord money thou haſt betrayed thy mayſter emonge alle thou choſen goo y• ſaraſyns grete truſt emonge al fydelyte thought thou haſt conſented trayſon allone haſt commyſed infydelyte fro whens cometh thyn inyquyte fals wylle plunged thabyſme auaryce thy naturel ſouerayn lord roulland olyuer haue doon yf thou haue wycked hate ayenſt one perſone wherfore conſenteſt thou deſtroye thynnocentes noo perſone thou loue deſt whan al cryſten men thou haſt ben trayter ony reaſon whan thou haſt ben capytayn ayenſt fayth auayleth proweſſe thou haſt made tyme paſſed whan thyn ende ſheweth thou haſt doo wyckednes fals auaryce ardeur concupiſcence fyrſt come •• myſchyef adam god dyſobeyſaunt noble cyte troye graūde put vttre ruyne deſtructyon thus thys manere ganellon brought gold ſyluer wyn wymmen rycheſſes tofore enterpryſed whan charles ſawe al thought al way doon good entent equyte wythout barat grete lordes knyghtes toke wyn charles took onely gold ſyluer moyen people took hethen wymmen themperour gaf conſente w •• de ganellon ſpake moche wyſely wrought ſuche wyſe charles alle hys hooſt paſſed porte cezarye ganellon dyd hym vnderſtōde kynges aforeſayd wold become cryſten baptyſed ſwere fydelyte emperour anone ſent peple tofore came ryere warde ſente roulland olyuer mooſt ſpecyal hys ſubgettes wyth thouſand fyghtyng men founcyuale thenne kynges marfuryus bellegandus coūceyl ganellon wyth fyfty thouſand ſaraſyns hydde wode abydyng awaytyng frenſſh men abode ij dayes two nyghtys deuyded theyr men two partyes firſt put xx ſaraſyn • put xxx thouſand ſaraſyns ¶in haunte garde charles xx thouſand cryſten men whyche anone aſſaylled wyth xx thouſand ſaraſyns maad warre ſuche • wyſe conſtreyned withdrawe fro mornyng vnto houre tyerce ſeaced fyght ſmyte wherfore cryſten men moche wery nede reſte theym neuertheles dronken wel good ſwete wyn ſaraſyns moche largely many dronke went laye • oymem ſaraſynoys alſo wyth brought oute fraunce wherfore wylle god ſhold al dede thende martyrdom paſſyon myght cauſe theyr ſauacyon purgyng ſynne anone thyrty thou ſand ſaraſyns cant ſecōd batayl vpon frenſſh men ſoo impetuovſly al dede ſlayn gxcept roulland baulduyn thyerry ſlayn dede ſp ••• ſomme flayn ſōme roſted quartred ſubmyſed many tormentes whan thys dyſcomfyture doon ganellon charles alſo tharchebyſſhop turpyn whych knewe nothyng werke ſo ſorouful ſauf onely traytre whyche ſuppoſed alle deſtroyed put deth ¶of languyſſhe comyng charles wyſte ſone comyng deth kyng marfurius roulland hurt wyth foure ſperes mortally al peple ſlayn capitulo ij bataylle haue ſayd tofore moche ſharpe whan rolland whyche moche wery retorned recountred hys waye ſaraſyn moche fyers blacke boylled pytche anone took hym thentre wode bonde hym tree ſtraytely wythoute doyng hym ony harme took rode vpon hylle ſee hooſt ſaraſyns cryſten men fledde ſaw grete quantyte paynyms wherfore anone ſowned blewe horne yuorye moche lowde wyth noyſe came hym hondred cryſten men wel arayed babylled wythoute moo whan come hym retorned ſaraſyn bounde tree roulland helde hys ſwerd ouer hym ſayeng ſhold deye yf ſhewed hym clerely kyng marfuryus yf ſo wold ſhold deye ſaraſyn contente ſware ſhold gladly ſaue lyf ſoo brought hym wyth hym vnto place ſawe paynyms ſhewed rolland whyche kyng whyche rode vpon rede hors certeyn tokenes thys poynt roulland reconfermed hys ſtrengthe truſtyng veryly myght god name iheſus lyon entred bataylle emonge encountred ſaraſyn whyche gretter ony gaf hym ſo grete ſtroke wyth durandal vpon hede clefte hym hys hors two partes one parte went one ſyde ſyde wherfore ſaraſyns ſoo troubled abaſſhed myght puyſſaunce rolland alle fledde tofore hym thenne abode kynge marfuryus wyth fewe fo • ke thenne rolland ſawe thys kyng wythoute fere came hym put hym deth incontynēt alle hondred cryſten men wyth roulland thys recountre •• erouſ • holyly many martyres oryſons made god ful deuoutely complaynte maad hys ſwerde durandal capitulo iij rolland valyaunt champyon cryſten fayth moche ſorouful cryſten men cauſe noo ſo • moche wery gretely abaſſhed moche affebled hys perſone loſt moche blode foure mortal woundes whyche leſte ſuffyſaunt hym haue deyed grete payne gete hym oute fro ſaraſyns haue lytel commemoracion god tofore ſoule ſhold departe fro body ſo moche enforced hym came fote montayne nygh porte cezarye brought hym ſelf nygh roche ryght roncyuale vnder tree fayr medowe whan ſat doun grounde byhelde hys ſwerde beſt euer named durandal whyche moche ſay gyuyng hard ſtroke whyche ryght fayr rychely made handle fyn beryle ſhynyng meruayllouſly hye fayre croſſe gold wryton name iheſus ſo good fyn ſonner ſhold arme faylle ſwerde took y• ſhethe ſawe ſhyne moche bryght cauſe ſhold chaunge maiſter moche ſorowe hert wepyng ſayd thys maner pytouſly ¶o ſwerd valure fayreſt euer thou neuer fayr ne neuer fonde good thou art long meſure thou haſt ſo moche honoured alwaye thou bareſt name bleſſyd iheſus ſauyour world whyche hath endowed wyth power god may comprehende thy valure ala ſhal haue ſomeuer hath ſhal neuer vaynquyſſhed alwaye ſhal haue good fortune ala ſhal ouer ſay good ſwerde many ſaraſyns haue ben deſtroyed thynfydels myſcreauntes haue ben ſlayn name god exalted made path ſauement many tymes thynge ſwerde clefte rocke therthe coude wyſe breke ſwerde whan ſawe facyon coude nomore therto took horne whyche yuorye moche rychely made ſowned blewe moche ſtrongely ende yf ony cryſten men hydde wodes waye theyr retournyng ſhold come hym fore wente ony ferther fore rendred hys ſoule thēne ſeyng none came ſowned ageyn ſoo grete force vertu ſo impetuonſly horne roof ſondre myddle vaynes hys vnderſtonde byleued hym made none ſ •• blaunte neuertheles rolland beyng thys ſorowe • e peaſed hys woundes alſo wel myght ſtratched hym ſelf graſſe freſſhenes forgete hys thurſt whyche ouer grete al ſtratched medowe began ſay thus fayre lord god maker redemour ſone gloryous moder comforte thou koweſt myn entencyn thou knoweſt haue doon bounte thy grete mercy whyche thou art enuyronned grace whyche haboundeth meryte thy paſſyon holy bytter good humble hert requyre y• tofore thys day faultes ſynnes ygnoraunces may pardonned take noo regarde treſpaces haue doon beholde deye fayth thou haſt byleue loue aboue loue neyghbour ¶o good lord beſeche pardonne forgyue alle theym thys day ben deed companye may ſaued alſo maker requyre take hede pacyence iob moche better deye thurſt allone wounded
